Rev. Sun Myung Moon's Words Compilation Committee

Foreword
                   President of the World Peace Unification Family, Hwang Seon-jo

1)
Reasons and Basic Direction for Organizational Restructuring
June is an important month when viewed in light of the historic providence centered on the Unification Church. 
The year 1971 is a significant year marked by historical importance, as mentioned by the leader. 
In June of 1971, until the lunar month of July, I believe it is a crucial period for our Unification Church. Therefore, as you know, we have restructured the association's organization today, on the first day of June. 
Reasons for Restructuring the Association's Organization and Church Structure
Until now, our church's organization included a headquarters, districts, regions, and local churches beneath them. This time, we have modified it so that the headquarters can directly oversee the entire church. By abolishing the district system, the district leaders have also become church leaders.
You may have heard through your church leaders, but in 1960, there were headquarters churches and local churches, and the headquarters church directly guided the local churches. Then we transitioned to a district system. In this system, if the district leaders fulfill their responsibilities, it may work, but when they fail to do so, issues inevitably arise at the church level. Therefore, today, on the first day of June 1971, we are restructuring the entire organization.
There are churches in the provincial capital, cities, towns, and villages. From now on, church leaders must exert their full efforts in their activities. If they have many capabilities, they should devise a system that allows for development. Among the church leaders, there will be town church leaders and village church leaders. Thus, each church leader must take responsibility for their own church and expand the principled structure in that area. Since the principle is an organizational form of the four-position foundation, we aim to establish a foundation centered on one main church. When the number of worshippers exceeds 40, it will be recognized as a church.
In this way, without regard to time, church leaders who quickly expand and develop churches in four locations will be promoted: a village church leader will become a town church leader, and a town church leader will become a city church leader. Additionally, when a provincial church leader secures churches with 40 members in four locations and fulfills their responsibilities, they will be appointed to important positions such as department heads at the headquarters.
Therefore, until now, district leaders and below, including regional leaders and church leaders, should not rely on anyone but will find their own paths based on their abilities and the results of their activities.
Establishment of a National Circuit System
We have also established a national circuit system at the headquarters. This system creates circuit members to manage churches across the country. We will have eight male and eight female national circuit members to mobilize maximum agility and ensure that the headquarters oversees the entire local areas, including counties, towns, and villages. This way, we believe we can visit local churches at least twice a month.
Until now, regions were under the district leaders, making it difficult for them to visit once a month. In some areas, there were places that could not be visited for three months or even six months. From this perspective, it has resulted in significant side effects on the development of our church, which is why we are implementing this restructuring. The fundamental activity of the church should be led directly by the headquarters to move the local areas forward.
Until now, evangelistic activities of the church were conducted by individual churches. The district headquarters or regional headquarters would set up a 40-day evangelism period, but from now on, the headquarters will oversee the entire nation. If there is a 40-day evangelism period in the future, local churches will submit their lists to the headquarters, and they will feel they are being directly assigned by the leader, as was done in the 1960s under special commands from the leader. They will also be connected directly in their devotion to heaven.
In the past, there were instances where specific tasks sent to the district headquarters did not reach the regions and remained with the district. Occasionally, there were cases where the district leader had a poor relationship with the regional leader, causing the regional leader's requests to never reach the headquarters. However, such occurrences will no longer happen.
But what problems arise when we create local circuit teams? If we fix the circuit team to a certain area, there is a concern that it may create tendencies similar to the past with eight district leaders. To correct this, we plan to rotate the circuit areas every three months. This way, the headquarters will receive reports from one circuit team for a district, and after three months, they will receive reports from a different circuit team. Thus, in one year, we will receive reports from four different circuit teams for that district, so if an incident occurs at a church and the reports do not match, the circuit team that provided the inconsistent reports will be held accountable.
By doing this, we can prevent the issues that have arisen in the past with the circuits and district leaders. Local churches will be able to report on the visits of circuit members every six months, as well as provide reports and suggestions on overall activities. This is necessary because we need to understand whether a circuit member has brought positive or negative results during their visit. Therefore, we have established a system for reporting these suggestions to the headquarters every six months. Starting from the 1970s, we must move forward with a new system.
Until now, district leaders have been positioned as if they were in a higher class, which has caused considerable controversy. District leaders have stood in a position where they do not execute the tasks sent from the headquarters but only direct the regional leaders. This has prevented those responsible for the system from demonstrating their responsibilities. From this perspective, if the circuit members sent from the headquarters go out and set an example, we believe that churches across the nation will gain new strength and develop, which is why we have chosen this structure.
Activity Direction Following the System Change
From now on, the headquarters must operate independently. By doing so, while church leaders could manage without fulfilling their responsibilities until now, they will no longer be able to do so.
The church leaders and members of each church must unite and cooperate to focus on church development; otherwise, they will fall behind. In the future, since everyone will have such a system, church leaders themselves must be active. In the past, even if district leaders did not act, if regional leaders were active, results could be achieved, but this will no longer be the case. Each church leader must be active for results to manifest, which is different from the past when the prestige of district leaders was built on the results of regional members or leaders' activities. Therefore, it is important to recognize that now each church must operate in a competitive manner.
From now on, the headquarters must seek various conditions both internally and externally to demonstrate agility. To solve these issues, we may need to purchase vehicles. The headquarters must bear all the expenses involved in this.
I hope you understand this and that from June onwards, we must move forward with new resolutions and new hearts. Just as all things grow centered around June, we must take this June as an opportunity for new development, which is the perspective the leader envisions for this June.
Furthermore, with this organizational restructuring, we must directly engage with the church leaders of local churches. In the past, if there were issues in the church, suggestions were made through district leaders, but from now on, they can directly suggest to the headquarters. However, suggestions should not be made arbitrarily but through national circuit members. Therefore, one concern is whether the national circuit members and national evangelism members, who will not work together for one or two years but will be replaced every three months, can achieve a unified heart. To address this, the headquarters will connect department heads with national circuit members to ensure normal national circuit activities.
Unite and Strive for Church Development
By restructuring the association in this way, I believe that church leaders and members across the nation, taking on new responsibilities, will march forward to achieve results that do not fall behind any local area or church. Therefore, I urge you all to unite and strive even harder for the development of your churches.
Among the church leaders in Seoul, some will be changed this time. Members of each church should unite with the new church leaders and make the second half of 1971 meaningful in development.
I believe that if we implement this structure for about six months, results will emerge. This time, the circuit members are different from those in the past. In the past, circuit members visited in a supervisory capacity, but this time, we plan to push forward so that church leaders and members can unite and hold revival meetings through the circuit members.
Thus, the most important department in our system is the national circuit team. This will naturally weaken other important departments within the association. The association will focus on managing the tasks of the department heads. The association will compile statistics from the reports of circuit members and summarize the situations to disseminate them nationwide. This dissemination should be done through our publications rather than through documents. From now on, members at the headquarters will also operate in this manner.
Until now, members of our Unification Church have not been interested in the "Unified World." There is also a publication called "The Way of the World" that goes abroad, but there has been no interest in it either. Therefore, by restructuring the system, we aim to make the publication a means of communication with the headquarters so that anyone who wants to know the news from the headquarters must do so through the publication. Thus, we also aim to increase the level of interest in the publication issued by the association through this restructuring. If members do not subscribe to the publication, they will not be able to know the news from the headquarters or the church.
The only other way would be to find out through the circuit members, which would be insufficient. Therefore, in the future, we must utilize our publications in various ways to enhance interest and bring about significant development, which is the leader's thought.
Furthermore, the national circuit team must take over the responsibilities previously held by district leaders. Issues such as collection, reporting, and revival will be quite complex, and I believe it will take about three months to get on a proper track.
I hope that the members in Seoul will unite around the church leaders until the church is established and strive to become a church that does not fall behind other churches. 
2)
The Masters of Tomorrow
<Prayer> Today is June 6, 1971, Memorial Day. On this Memorial Day, I reflect on those who have been seeking the path of heaven and have always been filled with sorrow. Moreover, this morning is the first Sabbath of this month. I hope that this morning can be a time for us to pledge a new prayer before the providential will, marking a day of victory.
May you oversee all the circumstances of this nation and the world in the future. We understand that we are in an important process of establishing a new system and direction centered around this month. When I think that this nation and our church must become a church and nation capable of fulfilling the mission of inheriting the foundation you desire, I feel that we must take June 1971 as a significant turning point to pledge our loyalty to your will in a new direction.
In the midst of the complex world situation, I ask you, Father, to help us understand what the fundamental issues are in the path of life we are flowing through. These are the unfortunate ones who are seeking their own positions to secure the hope of tomorrow. There is no one in the present who can stand in a position of glory. Faced with a bleak future, humanity stands at the fate of having to tumble along with the despair of this world. Father, please have compassion on them.
Father, who has established your providence and love on this earth, is there truly a subject of mercy who can inherit your heart of goodwill? If there is such a man, please draw him near, and if there is such a woman, please raise her up and bless her. If there is such a family, I know you desire to establish that family as one worthy of eternal praise in your heart. If there is such a lineage, I understand that you have a deep desire to establish a nation centered around that lineage. If there is such a nation, we know that you wish to establish it as a nation that can inherit your holy mission, replacing the ties of heaven and earth.
When I think that there are so few who can grasp your high and precious heart of providence and love on this earth, I realize that although there are many denominations and many believers, they are so far from your heart of suffering. We must not forget the historical tragic heart of your providence when we offer our prayers before you, grasping your lonely heart.
We, who know that we must find something to establish a connection from one perspective, feel an even greater responsibility to protect the sanctuary, even if we have to struggle for it. 

In a world that must eradicate the chaos that is to come, if you have trustworthy sons and daughters, you must tirelessly work to achieve the world you desire, and above all, you must be filled with longing. Even though we want to find such sons and daughters in the countless churches and faith communities today, there are groups that worry about their own liberation and salvation, but there are no groups that take responsibility for the sorrows of this world and your sorrows while trying to take responsibility for tomorrow's battle and their own difficult circumstances. 

Since our Father is a pitiful being, those who wish to follow your will must walk a lonely path, and we must think about the fact that we cannot do without pouring out tears and heartfelt devotion. Therefore, we ask you, Father, to protect all the lives gathered here. Lead us from the path of suffering to the path of victory, and watch over the footsteps of those who are fighting, knowing that the struggle is for your will. 

Currently, we find ourselves in a state of being too lacking, unfaithful, and immature, realizing that we must expose our own selves. Your sons and daughters living on this earth know in their hearts how they should live, but they are unable to translate that into action. We ask you, Father, to look upon this unfortunate situation. We must critically examine ourselves in light of the solemn task that our actions and hearts must align, that our lives and ideals must align, and that our lives must align with the historical providence. 

When we think about the fact that the path of destiny you must weave is burdened with profound loneliness and that dark clouds of sorrow and pain block our way, we realize that we must become sons and daughters who comfort our pitiful Father. We know that you have been saddened by humanity, and we understand the situation of our Father who has borne the pain of fallen relationships. We must gain insight into our Father’s heart as He looks upon humanity, which has wandered like children who have lost their parents due to the fall, from a position that contradicts principles and truths. We must now understand that while our Heavenly Father is always in a position of glory and always presiding over blessings, He is in a position where He must become the master of grief and redeem it through the cross before blessings can manifest. 

We, in our unworthy state, bow before your presence. When we think about being a historically precious entity receiving your great grace while inheriting the sorrow of heaven, we discover our own shame as children and realize that we cannot hope for a heart of forgiveness and compassion. Our longing for a place where your love resides must arise earnestly. 

May we be your children who, even if we must endure all kinds of arrows, pledge to bear it before you. This morning, please protect your lonely children scattered across the nation, Father. Because we have known a different path, we must endure different hardships, and because we have felt a different heart, we must experience a different loneliness. Because we have taken on a different responsibility, we must fight in a different battlefield, and because we know our respective responsibilities to walk the path of suffering, we must also fall with that responsibility. 

May this time allow your descendants who follow your path to take that as a standard for their lives and make their own pledges. 

Father, please remember this small group gathered here. Among them, are there children whom you can visit, children you wish to bless? Embrace those who want to hold onto your heart and be enveloped in your love, and may this holy time convey your story, Father, we earnestly hope and desire. 

We know that the Unification Church has not perished and remains before you solely because of you, Father. To comfort our sorrowful Father, we must be concerned for you from a place of greater sorrow than others. Knowing that there is no one to stop the sorrow of our Father who has gone through the historical acts of sorrow, we have come out with hearts that worry about the will of our Father. Since our beginning was like this, so must our end be. We must not forget that we have sown in suffering, so we must reap results in suffering. 

In the historical 71 years of the Unification Church, please remember the young daughters who are on the front lines during this period, Father. If there are those who shed tears before heaven while carrying their own grievances and worrying about the mission of the church in this era, please forgive them, and if there are those who are struggling because they cannot fulfill their own mission, please protect them. May they fulfill their historical mission and become a bridge and a foothold for heaven's fortune to come upon this nation and people, allowing heaven's great work to be inherited by this people. Though we are unworthy, may we be a group that does not forget the connection of your sons and daughters who can bow down and seek forgiveness before you, Father, we earnestly hope and desire. 

May our bodies and minds become your sanctuary, and may we not become a group that, while flowing with history, becomes torn apart and loses direction, but rather, may we be a group that dedicates our hearts and bodies in place of your eternal descendants to reap the results of victory and happiness, leaving behind an eternal tradition in the historical age. Thus, we must become those who have no shame before the heart of the Father who wishes for a group that remains forever, and at this time, we offer our unworthy bodies before you, so please accept them. 

We earnestly ask and desire that this morning may be a time when we reveal ourselves before you, so that your heart of compassion may flow and we may be eternally proven and receive counsel in your eternal presence. 

Please bless the groups scattered across South Korea who are looking towards this place and praying. We know how fearful this place is. Pour out your love a thousandfold upon those who long for this place, and remember your lonely groups scattered around the world who admire this nation. We are appealing and praying before you, so please hear our prayers. Father, we know that our philosophy of life must be to overcome difficulties while believing in and following your will, which comes to pioneer our future. May we be a group that pledges to devote ourselves wholeheartedly and faithfully to this path, Father, we earnestly ask and desire. 

Please take charge of everything, Father. We hope you remember this morning as well, and we pray in the name of True Parents. Amen. 

<Words> The point we are currently in is a point where the past and future are connected. This is true for individuals, for the situation of our country, and for the situation of the world. When we look at God, who is realizing the providential will, He is also in such a position. 

The Importance of the Present
Whether we look at individuals, families, tribes, nations, the world, or the heavenly providence that governs the universe, today’s position must be one that can prove the past and establish the future. Only then can tomorrow be more hopeful than today, and the future be happier than the present. This goes without saying. 

In this regard, we must recognize how important our current selves are, that is, our position as we live today. Depending on how today is, the question of whether the past shines or does not shine is determined, and whether a better future can be built because today exists or cannot be built is also determined. 

Therefore, to build a better future, the present must not be inferior to the past. Furthermore, those who cannot achieve victory in the present cannot be heirs who will remain in history. Those who cannot achieve victory in the present cannot become the successors of the future. When we speak of victory, if we become a group that cannot pledge the victory of the present over the victory of the past, we will be organized with the times. A group that cannot secure victory in the present cannot inherit the world of future victory, and it goes without saying that they cannot become a foundation for that world either. From this perspective, we must understand that we, who are alive today, are in an extremely important position. 

Those who disregard the present ultimately stand in a position that disregards the connections of the past, and those who do not value the present cannot stand in an important position for the future, which goes without saying. Therefore, we must always think that the present is the most important point in our lives and that the present is the decisive point that can determine our destiny. 

When a person fails, the point at which they can reaffirm success based on the results of past failures becomes an important period. That period is determined by a moment of today. We must not forget that our current position is faced with such a critical situation. If we fail today or if we take a misstep on our path today, no matter how glorious our past was or how brilliant our victories were, we cannot avoid a difficult fate in the future. This is something we can easily understand from everyday life or historical facts. 

Those who are irresponsible today cannot be held accountable for the future. If one has exceeded the standard of their destiny in the present, they must also exceed the standard of their life. Those who are not serious about the standard of life will not be able to remain in a future world that is more serious than the present. Those who are not serious today will not be able to remain in the future and will inevitably be removed. Since the complex environment of the present is related to the future, a group that cannot take responsibility for and overcome that complex environment will not be able to remain when a more complex future approaches, which is beyond question. 

Therefore, whether the past was precious or whether the future will be precious, even if the past is precious and the future is precious, and even if I have become someone who knows their value, if I cannot connect the past and future to the reality of destiny and reveal their precious value, both the past and the future must be condemned. Thus, we must feel that reality is a precious factor that can be a decisive factor for failure or success. 

Seek the Factors of Happiness in the Present
What one says and does in reality is not only related to the present. It is an action and word that can testify to the past and future. Therefore, we must speak words that newly proclaim the wrongs of the past in reality and take actions that guarantee and prove that the future will not be wrong. 

When everything we say and do in reality does not remain merely as reality but remains as sufficient content that can be more necessary for the future, that reality can govern the future, can become a standard for the future, and can also become a point that brings forth the light of the past. If there is a sad history in the past, it can become a point of hope from which we can settle that sad history and start anew. When we look at it this way, we can naturally understand how much we must value reality. 

No one wishes to fail in life. No one wishes to end their life in unhappiness. So, in a position where one wishes not to become unhappy or fail, at what point does that get determined? It is not in the past, nor in the future, but in the present. The motivation and key to rise and fall lie in the present. Rise and fall are not determined by the past or the future, but are decided in the harsh and cold process of time that is the present. Yet, we have not realized how serious this reality is. 

Thus, the responsibility that must be borne in the serious position of reality is not only a responsibility that remains in the present but also a responsibility that remains in the future. Moreover, we must realize that reality can be a good chance to settle the shortcomings of yesterday or the factors of past failures. 

Where are the factors of rise and fall? They are in reality. If one stands in a fate that can fail, the way to remedy that is neither in the past nor in the future. Therefore, those who cannot find this way in reality cannot become someone who can promise the future, no matter how much they resolve to do so in the future. In light of this issue, we can see that the most precious thing is reality. 

You must decide your central position from that realistic standpoint, as you are in a central position that can influence the inner and outer contents, so you are seeking happiness in reality. However, that happiness is not found by chance. You must first understand this. 

Those who live sorrowful lives day by day wish for a happy day. So, where should the factors for happiness be established? Of course, they must be established from the past, but even if they are established from the past, those who seek happiness without a solid foundation in reality to illuminate it are foolish. Furthermore, even if one is in a position where they wish for the future to be different while the present is like this, if they stand in a place where they have lost the motivation to find it in the present, they cannot guarantee future happiness either. Where is the motivation to settle the conditions that were happy in the past and to start the happiness of the future? It is in reality. Therefore, we must recognize that reality is harsh and merciless. 

If one missteps in a word in reality, that word can cause their entire life’s fate to waver. Moreover, if one missteps in an action, that action can become a factor that destroys and collapses the foundation of reality, not just flowing away. Thus, if past faith practices do not relate to today’s reality and do not shine in reality, then no matter how brilliant the faith practices were in the past, they have no relevance to today’s self. Also, if one thinks, “I am like this in reality, but I will be like this in the future,” while having the ability to create a foundation that can determine the factors for victory in the future, if they have lost the foundation to feel the factors of happiness from an internal standard, they cannot guarantee future happiness either. Therefore, reality is the most important. 

Those who forget reality stand in a position that denies the past, and those who do not value reality stand in a position that denies the center of the future. When we think about this, we realize that reality is indeed the most important thing for us. 

To Become the Master of the Future
Where, then, will the future's owner be determined from? Of course, it must start from the past, but no matter how well the starting point was and how well things have gone until yesterday, if one does not stand in the joyful position of confidently inheriting the factors of victory in today's reality, and if one does not possess the reality of victory or inherit the foundation of past victories, one can never become the owner of the future. Furthermore, if one does not have a position in reality that surpasses the past, a position that can illuminate the past, one cannot establish the criteria to inherit the foundation of future hopes. When we consider this issue, we come to realize that reality must indeed become the resurrection of the past.

Today, Christianity emphasizes resurrection. It stresses sacrifice and the need to be renewed every day. However, can one simply hope and wish to become such a person tomorrow? No, one cannot. That hope must be experienced within the realm of today's reality, meaning that one must integrate with the feelings of reality and create the conditions that can connect with tomorrow's life. A person who has lost this empirical foundation cannot become the heir of the future. Therefore, the foundation for becoming the owner of the future must be established from reality.

From this perspective, the question is whether the reality of oneself stands firmly in a position that can inherit the future. Reality must stand as a subject with the rightful authority to negate the past. Therefore, if one has a shining past, the question is how to discover oneself who can say that past existed for the present. The joy of past victors does not welcome the sorrows of today's losers. The pain of today's losers or those suffering as the weak cannot be accepted or inherited by the future, and when we see this, we realize that today is a time that cannot be overlooked. We can also recognize that one can become the subject of the factors that can make one the owner of the future.

Where will the owner of the future emerge from? It cannot emerge from a position that has lost today. When we look at the society we belong to, even if it is a corrupt and evil world filled with death, it is based on this evil world that we must inspire the future world. Today, a person who can remove the authority of this dark world within their realm of life, who discovers the subjectivity that can do so and lives with the determination to achieve it, is the one who will inherit a promising path in the future. Even if one is in a bleak position today and places all hope in the future, dreaming the biggest dreams, it is of no use. Since the future is determined through the reality process, one cannot find the foundation to inherit the future while standing in such a position. Therefore, we cannot underestimate how precious today is.

Is the past precious, or is today precious, or is the future precious? It is not that the past is precious, nor that the future is precious; today is precious. Therefore, you cannot deny that the reality you are struggling with, centered around sad moments, pain, unhappiness, or happiness, is the most serious and important. You all know very well that you must overcome the suffering environment you are in and strive to surpass this suffering environment.

This applies not only to friendships but also to social activities and dealings with the nation. Today, a person who can proudly stand before friends, as a member of society, and proudly stand before the nation can lead the era forward. Without such people and without the foundation of such an environment, we cannot meet a world of hope better than the present, nor can we find a starting point for a new beginning on this earth. When we consider these issues, you must understand that today is the most precious.

What must we do to have a reality that we can call joyful? We must not become people who retreat from the position of historical failure. It goes without saying that we must not become people who avoid the painful suffering of the future that approaches us.

When we reflect once more on the path of restoration, we can clearly see whether our ancestors have pledged victory before heaven or have stimulated the factors of failure, thereby increasing heaven's sorrow. Noah, who was so loyal and worked so hard before heaven, Abraham, who stood in a position of completely denying himself while forgetting his sorrow with a single-minded devotion to the will, Moses, who led the charge as an action-oriented person concerned about the fate of the nation of Israel and the future, and John the Baptist, who denied even the precious youth of his life to live a monastic life in the wilderness—when we consider whether they became the factors of victory in the historical era, we can see that they left behind the factors of sorrow as losers and did not firmly establish the foundation of victory.

Looking at this historical fact, we see that they walked the path of suffering for decades or even their entire lives. But how did such results appear? It is because they did not continuously have serious moments that could inherit God's providence in the reality they faced. Thus, we cannot deny the fact that the factors of failure emerged as a result of this.

In this light, we must stand in a position more serious than anyone else in the reality that has inherited the historical era. Moses, who was in a serious position for the nation, had a heart that desired to be the heir of the kingdom of heaven, hoping to establish Israel. We must grapple with the question of how to connect reality with the future from a position that worries about the fate of the future nation. Let us think about Abraham. He acted to eliminate all the conditions for his happiness centered on God's command, but in the end, he left behind the factors of failure and sowed the seeds of historical resentment. How did this happen? It was due to the very small mistake of not splitting the dove when offering it on the altar. In terms of time, it was nothing more than a tiny moment, and in terms of action, it was a very simple act.

In that tiny moment, he made such a great failure. While it was nothing in reality, it became the motive that turned the entire history upside down. Abraham did not know that this would happen. Unbeknownst to him, the factors of rise and fall were intertwined with the path of destiny in reality. When we analyze the painful factors of past failures, it is undeniable that we cannot correct the history that left behind the factors of failure without discovering ourselves who can boldly step into a position more painful than the past's suffering.

From this perspective, the reality we are in is the most serious moment. Therefore, the more we understand the intentions left by our ancestors in the historical era, the more we must think about how to determine our own position in the present, pledging to find an even more serious position than that. Moreover, to inherit happiness in the future, one must go through a path of suffering that is greater than the present. Thus, one must be the protagonist who can willingly face suffering greater than the suffering one is currently experiencing and can navigate the path of present suffering; otherwise, one cannot become the heir of the future or be born as a subjective being who prepares the foundation for the future. There is no need to say more about this. The future will present even more serious problems than the past.

Always be serious.

Restoring the individual comes before restoring the family in the path of restoration. Since the family is a greater foundation than the individual, it must be restored with a more serious content. Restoring the tribe is even more serious than restoring the family. To restore the tribe, one must go through a path of suffering that is more difficult than the suffering endured to restore the family. There are even more challenging contents involved in fulfilling the will that will be inherited in the future. Additionally, restoring the nation requires greater effort than restoring the tribe, and restoring the world requires even more significant effort than restoring the nation.

However, considering that the Unification Church has created the conditions for the established church to come through decades of historical processes, I believe this presents a historical standard.

As the glorious day approaches us due to the hidden merits of the Father who looks upon us with pity, we cannot spread our knees before the Father nor lift our heads. We humbly hope for the day of victory to be proclaimed and that many humble sons and daughters among the members of the Unification Church will be able to declare that they are true sons and daughters.

Father, please remember Your young daughters who are fighting on the front lines. As far as our hearts can reach, may You add more devotion before them, and protect their sons and daughters and their families. We know they will become a group that will never fail. We earnestly ask that they may endure until the end and become families that remain.

Even while fulfilling the mission of overseas evangelism, even while having a miserable life in foreign lands and among different ethnicities, may they remember the Father's hard work and strive to comfort the Father. We earnestly ask that You show them the connections that remind them that they are a group that will not fail.

May we be a group that can prove that the master of tomorrow is here, as the Father guarantees, and may we be allowed to be a group that can testify to this. I ask this again, and I offer all these words in the name of the True Parents. Amen.

We gathered

We must realize that we are not meant to live like this as humans, but to follow the path that heaven walks, to work with heaven, to live with heaven, to fight with heaven, and to be born to fulfill the will of heaven. This morning is the second holy day of June, so Father, please be with us at this time. The reason we have gathered like this is not for anything human.

We have come to know that the path we walk is one that no one else can take responsibility for. We have come to understand that establishing this nation before you cannot be done by anyone but us. <Words> There are many nations in this world. We know that there are countless countries with different ethnicities and historical backgrounds on this earth. We also understand that these nations, as they have different ethnicities and environments, have different national views and worldviews, and are walking different paths. Just as each nation is so, each individual living in those nations is also walking similar paths.

When we look at an individual, there is a path that individual walks. Just as an individual lives with the question, "What do I hope for and what do I live for?" a nation also carries the question of what purpose it must achieve in the face of its era. The same applies to the world. The question arises of what the world will do and what purpose it will achieve. Furthermore, if God exists, the question arises of what God will do and what purpose God will achieve.

People's hearts are drawn toward something more precious and valuable. Everyone wishes to succeed, but no one desires a success that is limited to themselves, solving only their own happiness. Achieving one's hopes, of course, includes wishing to unite with the hopes of one's kin, and if there is a nation, one wishes for the nation to align with the path they are taking to achieve the same purpose. This is a desire that everyone wishes for.

In this way, anyone wishes not only for their nation but for the entire world to unite with the path they are taking. If God exists, the same applies when viewed from the perspective of God. They wish for their path to align with a purpose that can please God. They hope to establish a relationship from the individual to the whole, sharing the same motivation and managing the environment to achieve a single purpose. This is a hope that anyone, regardless of their status, wishes for. When viewed this way, regardless of who it is, what they wish for in the morning, what they wish for during the day, what they wish for in the evening, and what they wish for in their dreams is all for the joy of the world. This is human nature.

So what is goodness? What is good? It is not something that only I can rejoice in, but something that can bring joy to my family, my nation, my country, and the world. Moreover, if God exists, it is something that can bring joy to God as well. When such things appear on this earth, it should not only be known by me but also be known by the nation, and not only known by the nation but also by the country, and after the country knows, the world should know, and after the world knows, Heaven should know. It should not be that I alone know and rejoice, but rather that the joy is not limited to me but is expanded to the entire world. When such a foundation is formed, that foundation can only be a good foundation.

The Life of Jesus as a Historical Foundation of Goodness
Jesus Christ died in a position that was not good in his time. However, if he is good, he must manifest as a being who can be recognized by history, and his standard of goodness must appear in the historical era of the world. Furthermore, he must appear as a good result in Heaven and Earth, so that Jesus Christ can stand in a decisive position as a good life and a good personality who lived centered on the foundation of a good world.

When we trace the historical path of the providence of restoration, we see that Jesus Christ, no matter how difficult the path of suffering may be, did not succumb to the dominion of the environment as the essence of goodness. Instead, he restructured and organized the environment based on the standard of goodness, forming a progressive new worldview. Although Jesus Christ's life lasted only about 30 years, what he left behind, what he hoped for, and what he practiced became a historical foundation of goodness. That foundation was not accepted in his time because it was built in an evil world, but because it became the path humanity must take and the foundation of goodness that humanity must leave behind, we know that although Jesus Christ has left, the path he walked and the hope he had have been inherited in the hearts of humanity.

Jesus has gone, but centered on the foundation of goodness, a new group has gathered around the hope he desired. The group that has gathered has grown into the Christians scattered throughout the world today.

These Christians have a mission to fulfill the ultimate purpose that Jesus desired in this world today. When they have fulfilled their responsibilities centered on the national position, they must take responsibility from a global perspective, transcending national boundaries. If God's providence remains, they must fulfill their responsibilities within the realm of God's providence, and if there is a second desire and second promise that God has not been able to fulfill regarding Jesus, they must stand in a position where they can ask God to fulfill those desires and promises. In other words, Christians have a remaining purpose of goodness that must be achieved beyond the providential boundaries.

The Mission of Christianity and the Purpose of Judgment
That is why it has been said that there is an end to the path of Christianity. What kind of day is that end? It is not the end centered on the kingdom of hope that Jesus desired. It is because the world, nations, and ethnicities that were in opposition to Jesus' hope must see the end of their nations, the end of their countries, and the end of the world. However, to see the end of the world, countless nations must overcome their ends, and to see the end of those nations, countless ethnicities must overcome their ends, and to see the end of those ethnicities, countless families and individuals must overcome their ends.

Therefore, the end, the time of the global end, is when the world must overcome. It is the time when nations that were in opposition to the country Jesus desired are passing through. Passing through does not mean passing without consequence; it means passing through judgment.

It involves distinguishing between what has succeeded and what has failed, leaving behind what has succeeded and removing what has failed. What has succeeded is on the side of goodness. This goodness must be connected to the future world that is coming. If it is not that kind of content, it cannot be considered good. In other words, the goodness of the individual must be connected to the goodness of the family, the goodness of the family must be connected to the goodness of the tribe, the goodness of the tribe must be connected to the goodness of the nation, the goodness of the nation must be connected to the goodness of the world.

That is why when a specific person establishes merit centered on goodness, if that merit takes on a global character, even if the history of the world collapses, that merit will remain. Along with the flow of history, receiving the cooperation of Heaven's fortune, the foundation of the merit they established will remain as the center of the world, transcending the nation. We come to understand the practical realities of the saints who have remained in the historical process.

Therefore, as the end approaches, this world will not remain as the current world of death itself, but can be organized and resolved around something that can be found in the future. In other words, it will not be a goodness that is less than what this world desires, but a foundation of higher-level goodness that this world desires, and even if the world disappears, it will be organized by goodness that possesses values that can never disappear. We must understand that the necessary requirement in that process of organization is judgment, which is necessary to discern between good and evil.
Therefore, what is the responsibility and purpose that Christianity, which is spread throughout the world, must fulfill? Rather than focusing on the desires of any particular denomination, the global Christian community must unite to achieve the higher ideals that all of humanity aspires to. In other words, Christianity should not be driven by the limited desires that can exist within the realm of death, but rather it must move with the desire to inherit the heavenly ideals that God envisions, transcending those boundaries. Without this, Christianity itself cannot stand on the foundation of goodness that God desires in the future, and we cannot deny that it will find itself in a position that must be judged.

From this perspective, where should Christianity, which is spread across the world, be heading? Today, it is not about Presbyterianism being Presbyterianism itself. It is not about Methodism being Methodism itself. It should not be confined to the environment of any specific denomination, but rather it must transcend denominations and overcome the world that exists within the realm of death, moving toward the place that the world hopes for. Without establishing a central content that can achieve this, the foundation of hope for Christianity cannot remain.

In this regard, what is the place where the Unification Church should reside today? We should not remain within the historical environment that the world is flowing through today, but rather we should become a group that can be welcomed in the new historical era that transcends this history. To achieve this, we must decisively conclude the world of death and have the achievements that can guarantee our place in the world of hope. Otherwise, we cannot be the group that remains.

Unification Church members must become the group of hope. If the Unification Church, which advocates for the unity of Christianity, goes out to achieve its purpose as a denomination, it cannot achieve the purpose of Christian unity. Today, as a group that has the ideal of unity, we must take a position that asserts how the many nations of the world represented by Christianity should be. Without fulfilling the mission of being a leader, we cannot seek the path of Christianity, nor can we pioneer the living foundation of Christianity, which is something that goes without saying.

From this perspective, we, the members of the Unification Church gathered here today, must recognize that we are not a group burdened with a mission limited to the historical realm of today. In other words, we are not a group that has gathered to achieve the purposes of the fallen world, born as descendants of the fall and still having ties to the realm of the fallen. Rather, we are a group that has gathered with a new desire, new mission, and new purpose to cut off all ties with the world formed by the fall and to start a new ideological world with God as our motive.

Today, we must become a group that those struggling in the valley of death can say, "They are the only ones who can bring us hope." Or we must become a group of hope that countless Christians, who have lost their way and are in a state of despair, can say, "We cannot be without them."

In the current urgent situation, where the Republic of Korea must break through the extreme difficulties representing Asia and form a new national ideology, it must become a group of the Unification Church that it should emulate. Before the nation facing trials and tribulations, the Unification Church must present the message that "No matter what trials and tribulations there are, the group that overcomes and remains is the group of the Unification Church." We must recognize that we are a group gathered to bear that responsibility. Everything I eat and sleep for must be to achieve this purpose, and my very existence must be to fulfill this purpose. Without becoming such individuals, it is natural that we cannot surpass the standards of judgment in the end times of this world that we are looking at.

Our purpose is the salvation of families. In this regard, we, gathered here today, are not a group that has come together to achieve individual salvation. We are not a group that has gathered for my own happiness. We are not a group that has sought faith for my own comfort. I have come to this place because I have been elected to a representative position. We must be aware of this.

Today, we have stepped onto this specific path in a land where many nations live, without others knowing. We did not step onto this path in an environment that welcomes us, but rather we have walked this path amid the opposition of many people, which undoubtedly indicates that there was a different purpose behind it. Because there was a different purpose, we must go a different way and start a different environment, and if we conclude with the same purpose, we will become a group that perishes with that world when it falls. To avoid perishing with the world, our path must be different, our standing environment must be different, and our purpose must be different.

That is why our faith is fundamentally different. Past faith aimed for individual salvation. Until now, faith has been pursued to save oneself. Our faith must be fundamentally different from such faith. The content must be different. "To achieve the purpose of saving myself, I must abandon the world. I must abandon the nation. I must abandon the tribe. I must abandon the family. I must abandon myself." This has been the path pursued by religion until now. However, the path that the Unification Church is taking today is different. It is not about abandoning; it is about reclaiming what has been abandoned. The need for the individual is to find the family. The need for the family is to find the tribe. The need for the tribe is to find the nation. The need for the nation is to form a state. The search for that state is not for the state itself but to find the world. It is fundamentally different.

So, what is the foundation for forming a nation? It is the family. Therefore, we must aim for the salvation of families rather than individual salvation. In the past, we had a relative relationship with God from a vertical standpoint, but in today's era, we cannot maintain a relative relationship solely from a vertical standpoint. That is limited to me. Until now, our faith life has been limited to me. It should not be that way.

Equipped with vertical content, I must become the subject and become a vertical reality, and that reality must determine a horizontal relative foundation. This is different from how believers have lived their faith lives until now. The position that general religions have desired until now is different from the position that the Unification Church desires today.

A man alone cannot go to heaven. Therefore, one man must become one with one woman. For this, one Abel must unite with Cain. Thus, people need their counterparts. The Unification thought states that "Before becoming a couple, one must have the relative standard of a brother to be restored." In the past, this was not the case. It was said that believing in Jesus was enough. However, we are fundamentally different. We must become one with our brothers. How must we become one? We must die to our former selves before entering the Unification Church and become one. Without determining the relative standard that can allow us to become one, we cannot walk this path. This is the starting point of Unification thought.

One man must form a family with one woman. Without this, one cannot go to the world of unity. While past believers abandoned the family, they cannot go to heaven without reclaiming the family they abandoned and establishing it as a victorious family on a higher level. Just because one family is formed does not mean that one can enter heaven. One must form a family of unity.

Where must this family of unity be formed? It must be formed on this earth. When must it be formed? It must be formed before one dies. Without achieving this, one cannot become a citizen who can welcome the nation, nor can one become humanity that can welcome the world, nor can one become the heavenly people who can welcome the world of heaven when God's will is fulfilled.

So, how should one victorious family of unity be formed? It must not be a family of unity that stands on a foundation that has been removed and surrounded by the environment of suffering in the flow of history. Instead, it must be a family of unity that stands on a firm foundation that has the power to manage the swirling currents of history from a new dimension and can become the basis and womb of that history.

Without centering on this, we cannot change the fallen worldview. This was the blessing that God granted to Adam and Eve before the fall. That blessing should not end with the joy of Adam and Eve but should continue to be able to rejoice with the history that passes beyond Adam and Eve, even if thousands of years of history flow by. The decisive standard of victory should not only be for Adam and Eve but should also extend to become the decisive origin of forming world nations. This is not something that goes back and forth. It is rooted, becoming the foundation from which branches and leaves emerge, flowers bloom, and fruits bear. This principled standard cannot be denied. This is something that even God cannot divide. No matter how much anyone tries to divide it, it cannot be divided. There is no one who can separate that connection.

Therefore, the ties of father and child, husband and wife, or siblings cannot be separated by anyone. Among siblings born of the same parents, even if a younger sibling says to the older sibling, "You are not my brother," or the older sibling says to the younger sibling, "You are not my sibling," it cannot be denied. In the relationship between husband and wife, even if one presents negative conditions saying, "You have nothing to do with me," such conditions cannot be established in the world. The ties of father and child cannot be broken or separated, no matter what force is applied or what authority tries to destroy them. Having such ties is the principled foundation of the heart of the family of unity. As long as that foundation of heart is not violated, the world formed with that heart will remain forever. The standard where parents and children are united with that heart, and siblings become one, will become the standard for eternity and the foundation for forming nations.

The teachings of the principle state that if there is one brother, that brother must exist to fulfill this common purpose. The older brother must become one with the younger brother to be able to lift his face toward heaven. The younger brother must become one with the older brother to be able to lift his head toward heaven. Why? Because it cannot be based solely on vertical standards. One must represent the vertical standard and demonstrate vertical value based on the horizontal standard.

That is why all creations have dual purposes. They have the purpose of the heart and the purpose of the body, that is, the internal and external purposes. If those internal and external purposes do not become one, God cannot be present. What is the teaching of the principle of creation? A traditional standard cannot arise unless the subject and object are completely united. This is the teaching of the principle. From this perspective, it cannot be based solely on vertical relationships.

Looking at the restoration principle taught in the Unification Church today, Cain and Abel cannot welcome their parents unless they become one. To break away from the fate that is drawn into the world of death, one cannot do it alone. With the cooperation of the Triune God centered on God, one must completely establish the family of unity based on a vertical relationship. When I say that I am in a vertical relationship with Jesus and the Holy Spirit, I must be able to say, "I exist for Jesus and the Holy Spirit. I exist for God." This is the vertical standard that can represent the family today. The Triune God, centered on God, Jesus, and the Holy Spirit, means that I have become one with them, which signifies the internal determination of the family of unity in the vertical relationship.

But is that determination enough? If so, then there is only me, and there is no family. There is only me, and there is no nation. There is only me, and there is no world. This is the position of Christianity. However, it is not just about me. "I" must broaden the scope of the family of unity based on horizontal standards. To do this, one must live according to the standard of the life that Jesus and the Holy Spirit lived on earth.

The life of Jesus, who lived in the world of Satan and determined the central standard of the family of unity, has become the standard for the victorious family of unity. Therefore, today I must create a horizontal model of that family of unity. That is why I ask you to fulfill the mission of tribal messiah. Here, the term tribal messiah refers to a position that transcends the brotherly standard. It refers to a position that stands on the foundation of the family. Therefore, one must establish a horizontal object centered on the vertical standard. Why? To establish the condition that I stand in the same position as Jesus. Thus, I become the representative of Jesus and the substitute of the Holy Spirit, and from the horizontal position, I must create a realm of resurrection to become completely brothers. The relationship between father and child and husband and wife also emerges from here. This is the framework of the family of unity.

Because there is the content of the three great purposes, the coming Lord can stand in the position of finding brothers, can stand in the position of finding a wife as a bridegroom, and can stand in the position of parents. Why? Because when the three great purposes are established, the family of unity is formed, and this becomes an inseparable foundation, allowing the whole to be completed. We must walk the path of new salvation, going the way of the fallen human Cain and Abel to restore the brothers. Among those brothers, just as Adam had sons and daughters, there are both men and women.

When they all stand in the position of being completely restored as brothers, a new marital relationship arises there. A marital relationship cannot arise without going through the relationship of brothers. Furthermore, one cannot have children without going through the marital relationship. This is the path of restoration. Therefore, one cannot walk the path of marriage without going through the relationship of brothers, and one cannot walk the path of parents without going through the path of marriage.

Why must you seek out Cain? To find the path of marriage. Why must you seek the path of marriage? To find the path of parents. Why must you seek the path of parents? To find the path that God walks.
the only way to return to the original state. 

To achieve this, it must not occur in a vertical manner but rather in a horizontal environment. 

Seeking the connection of brothers in this way is to pave the way for couples, and seeking the way for couples is to pave the way for parents, and seeking the way for parents is to pave the way for God, that is, to create a path where God can come and go freely. Therefore, it is necessary to complete the expectation of the son-in-law centered on God. 

Here, the path where God can come and go freely must not end with the individual but must represent the nation, the world, and heaven. 

The path of restoration is a path that must deny the whole. 

If the starting point is smaller than the purpose, one cannot reach the intended destination. In other words, if the content of the motive is not more faithful than the result, one cannot achieve the result. Is that not so? What this means is that if the principled standard of the expectation of the son-in-law is aimed at finding the world, then the value of that standard must be greater than the global value. 

From this perspective, Jesus said in the Bible, "The value of one life is greater than the universe." Without passing through such a position, God has no way to go. Without a foundation to start from to fulfill His wishes and achieve His purpose, the world He aims for cannot emerge. What is the foundation of the motive that can start to achieve that purpose? It is the expectation of the son-in-law. 

The title of today’s message is "We Who Have Gathered." From this perspective, why have you gathered here today? There must have been many oppositions before you came here. You must have cut off the world's opposition that told you not to come. You must have cut off your country, your tribe, your parents, and even your siblings. You came after cutting everything off. Therefore, you are the only son. There is nothing left but you. Only I remain. Why must it be that way? Why must God push you into a position where only you remain? It is because of the need for restoration through indemnity. If something is lost, one must start from a position that is equivalent to what was lost. 

So where did we lose it? We lost it with Adam and Eve. So, is Adam two? He is one. Is Eve two? She is one. To say that only I remain means that it is a position of one. As a man, "I am one." As a woman, "I am one." You must go out to that position. You must completely cut off the unwanted world that you were connected to through the fall. 

This is the world, this is the nation, this is the ethnicity, this is the tribe, this is the family, and this is me. You must not become the "me" of this world. That is tainted by the fallen world. You must not become the "me" who carries the burden of national authority. That is tainted by the fallen world’s nation. It becomes that way. You must not become the "me" who cannot escape from the authority centered on this ethnicity. That is tainted by the fallen world’s ethnicity. Similarly, the tribe is also tainted, and I myself am also tainted. 

Therefore, Jesus said, "If anyone wants to follow me, he must love me more than anyone else." This means that one must love Jesus more than anyone else and must not recognize anyone other than Jesus. It means not accepting anything. "You must not know your parents, you must not know your siblings, you must not know your king." It means to deny everything. And He said, "Anyone who does not carry his cross and follow me is not worthy of me." It means to overcome oneself. Why is that? Because you yourself are within the realm of the fallen. 

The reason for being in a position of "only I remain" 

You must remain as only I remain, but you must not be alone. Even if you are alone, you must know that God is with you. Elijah, when he fled from King Ahab who worshipped Baal, prayed in despair, saying, "I am the only one left." At that time, God informed him that there were 7,000 who had not bowed to Baal. Although he was the only one left, he was not alone; there were co-workers. What does that mean? It means that in the position where only I remain, there is a group that can support me. 

Even when we look at ourselves, although I am the only one left, I am not lonely. God is there, and there are angels. A better heaven than the world I lost is waiting. embodiment of Satan. This is not the word of the founder of the Unification Church. It is the 
principle. If there is someone who judges, has that person gone through this principled process?

it is not possible that he started from the painful experience of imprisonment. Why? Because the 
servants did not fulfill their responsibilities.

Until now, the founder has been enduring painful hardships. He is substituting for the suffering of 
the people of this nation. This nation exists not because the current government is doing well. It

Then let us leave a time when we can say we have abandoned everything. Why have we left our 
husbands and children? It is for the nation. We have taken a position of having abandoned for the 
sake of the nation. It is centered on the nation. What must we do in the future? It cannot be just 
the nation. There will also be times when we must abandon the world again. This is not to lose the

That is why we, the members of the Unification Church, cannot complain about difficulties. The same 
goes for the leaders of the Unification Church. Do not have a decadent mindset that says, "Since I 
have taken on some responsibilities, the headquarters will solve everything for me." The headquarters 
is not helping. The help from the headquarters is not because they want to help; it is not because 
they are obligated to help. Those who have homes should not be helped. Based on this principled 
standard, the founder has not yet commanded or practiced. Do you understand what I mean? Therefore, 
from that perspective, if the founder is to hand everything over to you, he must first put you to 
the test. You must clearly understand this.

<Words> For believers who are going forth with purpose, it is of utmost importance to consider when they might meet God. 

Meeting Between God and Humanity
When one has a hope, meeting the object of that hope is an invaluable event, especially when the content of that hope is significant. When the hope one desires is not just for a generation but is a global hope, the time of meeting the subject of that hope is a historical moment.

When considering a nation, the time of meeting the historical figure that the nation hopes for is the most precious moment in the face of historical fate. When looking at the world, if the world is moving toward a certain purpose, meeting the one who can fulfill that purpose is an event of global significance.

Whether or not one meets the time of that encounter determines whether one can seize that opportunity favorably for oneself or for the whole. While people may wish to seize the right moment, doing so is not easy.

In terms of timing, if the opportunity that comes is at a national level, there must have been heavenly fortune in the process of traversing the path of destiny as a nation, or in the various processes that nation has undergone. If there were ten such moments, the question becomes how well that nation has matched those ten opportunities. If it matched eight out of ten well, the two missed opportunities would remain as sorrow.

Thus, in meeting the new time that is coming, God's desired standard of hope must be to atone for the past failures and to welcome this time more valuably than any time in history. God desires this and will come again to the nation that has not met the heavenly fortune in the past. If God comes again with the hope that this time will be better than any time before, but it does not go well, then the sorrow of the two missed opportunities from the past will inevitably be added to that failure. We cannot overlook such matters.

From this perspective, as we pursue the providence of restoration centered on God's will, we can see that there has never been a time when God did not seek to meet humanity. Each of you is in a different position due to the historical processes and traditions your ancestors have gone through. Therefore, God will surely come with the purpose of turning individuals who are in the realm of death into the realm of resurrection, based on the myriad circumstances of humanity and the individual personalities.

Thus, we must fulfill the purpose of God's coming and align ourselves with that will, standing in a position where we can be loved and praised in the presence of the hope God desires. When we meet Him in such an environment or position, God will treat us with joy. When He treats us joyfully, connecting us with joyful stories and concluding in joy, even if we part ways, we can do so with a heart that wishes to meet again, with a desire to meet joyfully once more.

In this way, God will wish to return to a place of greater value than the one we met Him in, and we, who have had the time of meeting, will leave that joy as a hope for the future. When we part from such a position, what kind of place will it be when we meet again? God will not want that place to be lower than before.
