At that time, just moving from this place to another would mean fighting. It meant fighting against global Satan. It meant glaring and grappling. Such things were happening.

However, now, no matter how gloomy and oppressive the place is, there is nothing to fear. No trivial matters come close, no matter where you are.

When children are throwing stones at the sea, if a big wave comes rushing in and collides with them, do the gentle waves break or not? It's the same. It changes drastically. Such things happen. You may not know it. This way, the direction is set, and it is gradually rising from the bottom. The Unification Church is rising from the end. If it has risen all the way to the top, everything caught there will flow away. Considering that, the current time is indeed a very good time.

The time of heaven is near, but the time of this world is complicated. It's contradictory. Do you understand? The external time is complicated, but the time of heaven is the starting point. Do you understand? The Republic of Korea is in the most complicated time, with opposition both internally and externally, including from the religious community and the nation, and it was at the very end that the Unification Church started. That was in the 1960s. Now, this has become the origin, and neither the church nor the nation opposes it, so it surpasses the external world. Why is that? Because we made atonement centered on the Unification Church internally. In the future, the Unification Church will advance toward the liberation of the world, facing both the democratic and communist worlds, centered on numerous religions. That time has come. It will surely happen in the not-so-distant future. Such conditions are unfolding right before our eyes.

In this light, it is now truly the time to enter the great sea. It is truly the time of the highest hope that individuals have longed for, the highest hope that families have longed for, the highest hope that nations have longed for, and the highest hope that both the democratic and communist worlds have longed for.

So, does that time come with a trumpet call? Does it come with a telegram? Has anyone received a telegram saying, "The April 19th uprising is happening"? Has anyone received a telegram saying, "The May 16th revolution is happening"? However, because people say it will perish, such things happen. A new tomorrow comes. After the winter solstice, what comes next? The spring breeze gently arrives. Whether you notice it or not, it comes, and after a day or two, you realize, "Ah, spring has come." When spring comes, the cold wind is unpleasant, and women don't want to go fetch water. However, in the spring, flowers bloom. Interesting domestic life unfolds. Similarly, while the world may oppose, the Unification Church itself must be in a position to welcome the blooming spring and engage in new domestic life.

If the time comes that individuals long for, that nations long for, that the world longs for, and that heaven and earth long for, then everyone will pack their bags and go out to meet that time. Don't you want that? At that time, if your son is the seventh descendant and you say, "I can't go because of him," then both will perish. At that time, you must say, "Hey, you must go. You must go." Even if you have to kick him out or drag him along, you must go.

When the Israelites were in Egypt, and Moses said, "It's time to leave. If you don't leave by the 14th, you will perish," what do you think they did? When asked, "Will you go or not?" the Israelites might have said, "We have suffered for 400 years in Egypt, living in an environment that is not lacking at all. Why would we miss our food? I want to live here." At that moment, Moses might have wanted to strike them with an axe. "You traitors to the nation..." he might have thought, wanting to beat them.

Would the Israelites have believed Moses when he said that the time would come for them? They might have thought that a thief-like world was trying to deceive them, and they would have said all sorts of things.

Thinking about that, behind the scenes, God might have sent a powerful force that would poke them with a spear if they didn't go. Would they have gone when they simply said, "Let's go, let's leave"? Since they didn't go, God had no choice but to bring down the ten plagues to create an atmosphere of fear and compel them to leave. He said they would perish if they didn't. Is this the work of God?

That's why the Israelites are still paying the indemnity for not having gone to the land of Canaan. God is doing all sorts of things to resolve the myriad of misfortunes that have accumulated behind the scenes. If this doesn't work, He tries that, and if that doesn't work, He tries something else to push that environment together and deal with it. So, is that meant to kill or to save? It is to save.

If you need to escape, but your baby is hungry and sucking on your breast, what should you do? Does the baby know about the evacuation? Does the baby know about the enemy troops? Does the baby know that the enemy troops are coming to stab people to death with pickaxes and spears? If a mother says, "I can't leave until the baby is done nursing," is she really a mother? At that moment, she is not a mother. She is an enemy. If the baby cries, you must cover its mouth and leave, even if you have to carry it upside down. (laughter) Even so, going to evacuate is the mother's mission. But is it love for a mother to say, "Oh, it's too bad the baby can't nurse"? A mother's love must have its limits.

Knowing this, can the Unification Church's True Father be oblivious? If a family has five children but can't survive, if the husband is sick, and the children are disabled, the True Father will still try to send the wife out. If she says she can't go, he will tell her to go with her eyes closed. That's how it must be. That is love. There are times when such things are necessary. You must realize that the time is now. Some people say that the Unification Church is telling women to evangelize, and they feel blocked, but it's fine if they feel blocked. That's the way of the Unification Church. The path of evangelism may be blocked, but the path of the world is open. The path of the nation is open. By the women of the Republic of Korea.

It's okay if the Unification Church fails. If about 1,200 people die so that the Republic of Korea can eternally ride the heavenly fortune, then that is what must be done. Those who die in that way are not perishing. Standing in a sacrificial position, they will have the opportunity to inherit the heavenly kingdom, which they could not attain even with a lifetime of loyalty. Such times will come. You may not know it, and your parents may not know it, but it is the time they have longed for, a time that your good ancestors also longed for, and a time that humanity today does not know but longs for. We are running toward that time.

Yesterday, I went to Cheongpyeong and drove a motorboat. I realized that if I keep the steering wheel level, it will surely go straight. However, if I move my hand just a little, the direction shifts. If I move my body, the boat moves accordingly. "Wow, look at this. Something that seems so trivial and unrelated is actually a decisive factor," I thought. I tried to turn the steering wheel forcefully. Everyone disliked it. Who would like that? Even those who were dozing off or dreaming disliked it.

When you turn sharply all at once, there are many sacrifices. The ignorant masses are sacrificed. If you turn the ignorant world sharply, there will be many sacrifices. Isn't that the time of judgment? That's how I see it. The wiser a person is, the more they secretly turn things little by little. The Unification Church operates in that way.

The Unification Church, which seeks to ride the heavenly fortune, has been criticized, and everyone has been shouting that it will fail, but it is looking toward the distant standard. When looking toward that distant standard, nothing close is visible. You must choose that standard and move forward. "Why are you going that way? That's wrong," they say, because they see it right in front of them. Just because something looks plausible in front of you, if you go that way, you will end up in ruin. Is that acceptable? To turn this world around, can we be like the people of the world? No, we cannot. So what must we do? We must walk that path. What kind of path is it? It is a miserable path. It is the opposite of the world. Without being connected to that path, you cannot achieve your purpose.

What kind of time will it be in the future? Among those coming to the Unification Church, there are people who say, "I served as a pastor in established churches for decades, yet the Unification Church doesn't recognize me. Why doesn't the person called True Father even greet me? Isn't that a lack of courtesy?" There are people who spread rumors about this. Do they not recognize me? Did they invite me because they liked me? Such people will say, "Now that I have become a member of the Unification Church, make sure I eat well." That is what they want.

They believe that the Unification Church should provide for their livelihood. If they live in Jeonju, they expect to be fed there. However, they say they will leave if they die. That's why I don't meet anyone now. The True Father is not someone who meets people like a neighbor when they need him. They might say, "What is this? You made a solid promise, and now you are acting like this?" But I promised to act solidly, not just to speak.

Look, the Unification Church must welcome the great fortune. So what must happen? You must not assert yourselves. Your assertions must dissolve and become leaven. You must be pure and swept along. When you are in the realm of entering the great sea, you must eat anything while playing in a way that aligns with that direction. Without doing so, you cannot welcome the great fortune, that is, the heavenly fortune.

If I say this, you might call me a fatalist, but there is a heavenly fortune. There is the fortune of the world, the fortune of the nation, the fortune of the family, and the fortune of the individual. When the family is in ruin, the individual suffers. Even in a happy family, if the nation falls, everything breaks apart. It is a destiny that can break at any time. No matter how well the Republic of Korea does, if the world turns upside down, it will be dragged in. Isn't that so?
Even if the fortune of the world is great, when the heavenly fortune swells, one gets swept away by it.  
Therefore, wise people follow the heavenly fortune. In a way, dreamers are religious people. Christianity says, "Our Lord will come in a few thousand years." Are those people sane or are they right? (Laughter) They say, "In a few thousand years, He will judge the world, strike down all the wicked, bring those we need, and create a nation and a heaven." When you ask when that will be, they say they don't know, but it will come. They don't know how it will come, but they say it will come. (Laughter) Thinking like that is absurd.  
What kind of person is a wise person? A person who can ride the heavenly fortune. We should ride the heavenly fortune. Everyone, is heavenly fortune good or bad? "It's good." Is Apollo 11 good or bad? "It's good." It landed on the moon, so that's good. But when it lands on the moon, does it just feel good? Is it just good? It's good because it can be good; is it just good as it is? "It's good because it can be good." If it can't be good, what happens? It changes one's fate. (Laughter) It's like floating around anywhere. You should be able to be good and feel good; if you say it's good when you can't be good, that's the end. It's the same. Therefore, we should ride the heavenly fortune.  
South Korea should also ride the heavenly fortune. The Unification Church is not saying it will ride the fortune of South Korea. What fortune should we ride? We must ride the heavenly fortune. Within heavenly fortune, there are trivial worker fortunes. There is individual fortune. There is fortune for sons. What fortune should we ride among those? "The fortune of sons." Among sons, there are good sons and bad sons. There are blessed sons and unblessed sons who are ungrateful. Do you think all sons are the same? They should become sons and daughters who can be blessed. Wouldn't that be good? We must walk that one path. That one path is the hardest path. Is it the hardest thing to skip a meal when others are eating?  
They must eat to live, but that son often goes hungry. People want to live by playing and eating, but that son often works to the bone. People want to live by receiving praise, but that son often receives insults. If he is praised because of his parents, is he a filial son or a disobedient son? If he received endless insults because of his parents, is he a filial son or a disobedient son? "He is a filial son." He is a filial son. Then, if he suffers endlessly for the country, is he a traitor or a loyal subject? "He is a loyal subject." If he suffers endlessly for God, would God say, "Hey, you suffered because you are useless. I don't need someone like you"? To ride the heavenly fortune, you must suffer endlessly. No matter how you think about it, that is the only conclusion. The best conclusion is only that. That is why the teacher is walking that path. It is a path of endless suffering. Everyone, you don't like endless suffering, do you?  
The Joy of Heartfelt Unity and Reunion  
When people meet and hold on to each other, some may think, "Well, we met," and hesitate to hold on, but eventually, some may hold on out of necessity. There may be such people among you. On the other hand, there are those who want to hold on and do so. Some may grab hands and embrace.  
So how do parents want to be held? If you hold them like that, do you think they will say, "What a strange thing! Oh, this is crazy," and hope to be held quietly, even if their newly worn dress gets torn? If the dress gets torn, so be it, whatever the situation, if others laugh, let them laugh.... What is more valuable? "Oh, can we do that for the sake of appearances? We have to be mindful." There may be parents like that. But that is not the issue.  
Opportunity for Reunion  
When parents are invited to observe students' learning at school, a student whose mother's face is a bit crumpled may sulk and think, "I wish my mother wouldn't come to school." (Laughter) Would a mother think about her daughter's face when she meets her? "Since I look this ugly, my daughter is not good enough." Are there parents who think like that? Regardless of how they look, they just want their daughter to be good. The mother may not think that way and just smile happily, but if the daughter acts embarrassed and says, "Oh, what kind of parent is that?" and ignores her, will the mother feel good or bad?  
However, no matter what anyone says, they should shed tears and say, "Mom is here." Children who don't know will say, "Oh, so that is so-and-so's mother. My mom isn't like that..." But teachers or those who understand the situation will say, "Wow!" The more young ladies and young men who support that child, the more that child becomes excellent. At school, they say, "Having such a student in our school is a pride." Wouldn't that be so? Would there be teachers who say, "Oh, having such a student in our school is not good"? Teachers who know that student's actions say, "So precious, so precious." That becomes a scene worth writing in a diary.  
Our Unification Church is the same. When I was in Seodaemun Prison, I was grateful that all the Unification Church members came to visit me. Are those Unification Church members a doomed group or a thriving group? If a husband ends up like that, when he goes to the prison, he might cover his face for fear of being recognized, but no matter where he is taken, he comes to visit. If someone asks, "Why are you here?" they say, "Oh, I'm here to visit Reverend Moon of the Unification Church." They fight to visit each other first. So, are those who fought to do so doomed to die in South Korea or will they survive? When I hear such words...  
Then, a warden or a chief comes and says, "Reverend Moon of the Unification Church is rumored to be a terrible person, but he is not." Then, about a month later, they come and say, "Teacher." They realize they are learning a lot. They are scolding because of the teacher, but are those who scold going to thrive?  
These days in South Korea, they say, "Corruption and decay. They are a band of thieves." What would the Unification Church say? Would they say they are worse than a band of thieves? Would they call it plunder? Would they call it ruin? Others steal to live well, but the Unification Church breaks down all the possessions and steps forward to save the country. They say they dance naked, but it is not dancing. They are stepping forward naked. But are they a doomed group? Absolutely not.  
In what position will you meet the time of reunion?  
So when you meet the opportunity for reunion, how should you be? Should you be dressed in fine clothes, eating rice and meat at mealtime, sleeping for more than twelve hours, about 72 hours, for about three days, wearing good clothes, and singing "Live for a thousand years" as you did when you were young, preparing to meet like this? If you do that, you will miss the time. Even if you are late, if you arrive one moment, not just one second, but one hour or three hours late, what will happen?  
Therefore, we must go centered on those who have walked the path of trials for humanity. When people are struggling and suffering, the world may say, "What kind of Unification Church group is that? May they perish!" But for the purpose, God calls such people.  
Then, will you meet in a well-fed and well-dressed position, or will you meet in a place where you bleed and collapse? If you meet while struggling, that person can inherit the heavenly thought for thousands of years and become a hero who can be praised as a subject of thought that can support that tradition for eternity. That is what I think.  
Then how will you welcome the new heavenly fortune that will appear in the future? Will you welcome it with a plump body? Or will you meet it in a state of being so emaciated that you are left with nothing but bones and become so weak that you cannot speak? You must meet in such a position.  
Even if the appearance is miserable, the internal story can melt the heavens and the earth and remain, having the active authority to turn the world of laughter into a world of tears that everyone can recognize. Isn't it the wish of all people to stand on such a foundation? Isn't it a more valuable thing? That is why I have not built the headquarters yet.  
How many Unification Church continents are there now? Have you counted? How many are there now? One, two, three, four, five, six. There are six continents. It sounds unpleasant. Six is the number of Satan so far, but since I am going ahead, it becomes seven, right? I think that way and want to indemnify it. That is how I think.  
You must clearly understand the time. How will you meet the time of reunion? You must meet in the most loving, most needed, and most valuable, unique position. Even if you have become wounded and impoverished to melt away all of your flesh for love, do not limit it. If the owner is surely the one who knows me, that owner will undoubtedly promise the world of happiness and prepare the foundation of blessing beyond the stories of a thousand years. Therefore, the question of what position you will meet the opportunity for reunion is now a problem you face.  
A few days ago, there has been a meeting of the members of the church, and yesterday evening I told them such words. "You will have a time in your life where you must meet the will of heaven, and do you know in what position that time will appear? That time may come through the hand of a beggar. Or it may come at the place where the final fate is determined, at a place of misfortune where a will is made. Or it may come through the hand of a crying baby, through the appearance of a baby. Even if you are in a position where you do not know when that longed-for time will come, if you do not have the mindset to prepare to meet that time in any environment, you will not be able to meet that one true connection that comes only once. If you miss the final chance that may come to you even in a place where you can only be sad, wronged, and die, how pitiful would I be? That is why the teacher endured while being beaten to meet that time and endured while walking the path of death." That time will come, and if there is someone who has that mindset, the path they take will open up.  
Let us move forward with hope to meet the global time of reunion.  
Jesus Christ said, "Abba Father, not my will, but your will be done." He understood that doing so was a golden opportunity to meet the final will of the Father that came to the earth and to establish a connection with the Father. That is why he had an aspect of denying his own will and trying to stand before the Father's will.  
What is that golden opportunity? Is it during sleeping time? Is it during mealtime? Is it during playtime? We do not know. That is why we must gladly accept the path of the cross. It cannot just be a joyful path. If we are too joyful, we will miss the time. We must find what kind of connection comes amidst that joy, day or night, we have been living to find that, haven't we?  
God has been working tirelessly for six thousand years. Wouldn't God, who works tirelessly, want to meet those who are tirelessly seeking to inherit His will? Such a person, even if they suffer in the position I mentioned earlier, seeks that time, finds that time even in joy, and seeks that time even in a place of death. If one is not such a person, they cannot be needed before God, who has been working tirelessly for six thousand years. When we think about this, we realize that our faith and aspirations so far have put us in a position that is too irreverent before God.  
In this light, what position will you meet the opportunity for reunion? This is the problem. Even if you become disabled, if you became disabled for the purpose, there is nothing to be ashamed of. There is no shame in becoming a disabled person who cannot use one arm. Even if you become a disabled person who cannot manage your own body, there is nothing to be ashamed of. If you have the desire to give even more, to dedicate your whole life, that person will remain forever. You must think about these things.  
Then, at this point, in a position to enter the mainstream, how will you harmonize with that fortune and align with the direction of that fortune? Will you be someone who is opposed to the flowing current or someone who is inevitably swept away by it?  
The trials and pains in such circumstances become blessings. That is why we seek God's compassion, the compassion of humanity, the compassion of history, and the compassion of the times, and if we can start from there, God's desire to find the world will relate to "me" or to the Unification Church. The place we are trying to reach is not a place of joy, not a place everyone looks at, not a place everyone welcomes.  
From this perspective, the teacher also thinks so. "There will come a time when the leaders of the Unification Church will oppose me. Not only that, but there will also be groups that will try to kill me." What will you do when you find yourself in such a position? Jesus did, and so did historical saints. Because they are rooted in a wicked world, all sorts of things happen. You must understand that the path that prepares for such problems is the teacher's path and the path of the Unification Church's mainstream. How will you meet in front of such a mainstream and path? This is the issue.  
If you have met, the connection of reunion does not end there. You must go to a higher place. If you met as individuals, you must meet as families, and if you met as families, you must meet as tribes. The teacher has always come out joyfully centered on the will of God, even in various difficulties. It is not always joyful to come out centered on the family. You must go through connections that can joyfully reunite centered on tribes, nations, and the world.  
As you think about how many times you have met the opportunity for reunion, whether it is personal, familial, national, or global, I hope you will resolutely move forward while looking forward to tomorrow's hope.  
<Prayer> Father, who am I, where am I, and what am I seeking? We must think about what flow of process your children who have gathered here are walking through. I feel that this is indeed a critical time.  
Recalling the 1960s when Unification Church members worked hard, the blessing of the Unification Church...
of the most tragic and desperate groups, I hope that they will not miss the opportunity for reunion in this remarkable historical era. I earnestly ask that you bless them so that they can engrave these words in their hearts and bodies, making them a turning point in their lives. I pray all these things in the name of True Parents. Amen.

**Longing for Hometown**

You all know that the place where the teacher's parents and siblings are located is Jeongju, North Pyongan Province. The teacher was a child whom his mother loved more than anyone else. 

The teacher's older brother had an illness but was healed through the power of faith, and he was someone who knew in advance through the spirit world that this country would be liberated. He had great expectations for his younger brother, even though he did not know what mission his younger brother had, and he came out with a hope greater than anyone else.

As a younger brother, I made him work hard. When looking at the issue of the restoration of the fallen man in the history of restoration, in that sense, my brother was a representative of the position of the fallen man. From the moment I was born, our family entered a path of hardship. No matter how difficult the circumstances were, my brother never complained about working hard for his younger brother. I never had a quiet moment to meet him and share feelings like I do with you.

On June 24, 1971, at the former headquarters church.

* This message was provided by Elder Joo Byeong-kyu (working at Ilhwa Co., Ltd.). The title was added by the editor.

Also, regarding our father, he was a man who could live without laws. If he borrowed money from somewhere, he could not stand not paying back even the interest on the promised day. No matter what happened, he was a person who fulfilled his promises. He was exemplary in fulfilling promises. He was a person who could live without laws. I have never had the heart to show filial piety to such a father.

Looking at my younger siblings, both my older sister and younger siblings were sacrificed because of the teacher. They were sacrificed both inside and outside. Considering all this, the teacher has left an emotional bond with the family that cannot be forgotten.

Moreover, I feel sorry for my mother... Some of you may know this. During the Japanese colonial period, there was an incident where the ship "Gonronmaru" sank. At that time, the teacher was supposed to be on that ship. He had sent a telegram saying he would go back to his hometown. But when he went to Tokyo Station to leave, the heavens blocked his way. At that time, three friends had come to see him off, and he was led to turn back... If he had taken the train and boarded the ship at that time, he would have been on the ship when it sank. Because of this incident, he ended up going to a friend's house. He had sent a telegram saying he would go to his hometown, but now he had to send a telegram saying he could not go...

"Well, since this happened, let's play together for a few days," he was pulled along by his friends and spent three days with them, and he did not send the telegram. Until then, he had not even thought that the ship had sunk. He found out about it three days later. He sent a telegram home, but during that process, there was great chaos in his hometown. The news was that the ship had sunk, and since the telegram saying he was coming home had arrived, they thought he must have died.

If a woman walks around without wearing a skirt but in underpants, that is not her true self, right? That's what his mother said. At that time, it was September, so it wasn't cold, but would she have had the mental space to think about shoes or anything else? When he thought about that, he felt, "Ah! This is what parental love is." The distance from the teacher's hometown to Jeongju is 20 ri. His mother ran that 20 ri barefoot and went to Busan, not thinking about God or clothes or anything else. She ran out barefoot because she thought her son had died and went to the Busan Fisheries Police Station to investigate, but he was not on the list, so how could she know? Therefore, his mother was convinced that her son had died, and as she became absorbed in that thought, she did not realize that acacia thorns had pierced her soles while she was running barefoot. She did not know it was infected and festering until it was too late. He returned about ten days later, and when he heard about that, he thought, "Ah! I was too harsh." That was his mother.

There were high expectations for the teacher in the family. They thought that once he graduated from school, he would become something. In that area, he was a controversial figure. If he succeeded, he would be a loyal subject, and if he failed, he would be a traitor... His personality was remarkable, and he was a man who generated such rumors. When he thinks about how great his mother's love for him was, he resolved to be filial to her, but he never had the chance to do so.

God has worked through me to this point. 

When the son graduated from school and returned home, he was headed for prison. Whenever he was taken away, it was to prison, so his mother came to visit him there, crying tears of sorrow, saying she thought he would become a dragon but had become a pupa. She heard all sorts of rumors. He is not saying this because he feels wronged. He felt bad about how his mother cried for him in prison. A mother who cries for her child must have her own stories, but he was thinking about God. Did his mother know that? She never said anything like that. His mother should have focused on God, risking her life to continue the historical tradition, blessing her child on the path he took, and encouraging him to walk the path of heavenly principles. Of course, his mother did not know this. But from God's perspective, it should not have been that way. It damaged his dignity and face. 

That is why the teacher told his mother, who was crying, to step aside with a thunderous voice.

He could not say a single word of the Principle to such a mother or brother. Why was that? Because he had to correct the path of Jesus. He had to resolve the resentment of Jesus, who could not share the circumstances of heaven with his own parents and relatives. He had to stand in a position more miserable than that. This was undoubtedly a path of blessing that could represent all humanity, yet if he had wept while holding onto his mother and father, and had taken the time to repent on behalf of everyone with a heart full of sincerity, his father, mother, and siblings would have protected his path more than anyone else. Whether it was his younger brother, older brother, or son, even if there were hundreds of deaths in the way, those parents and siblings would have endured all sorts of humiliation and sorrow to protect their child, brother, or son. The teacher left such a family behind and poured out his love on you, who are unrelated to him. This is undeniable.

In prison, he hoped for God's mercy centered on worthless death row inmates. Just as Jesus said to the thief on the right while dying on the cross, "You will be with me in paradise," he wanted to provide comfort to those who were walking a lonely path in misery.
For the sake of your son’s path, when the stories of tears intertwine through the sympathetic words of death row inmates, it is said that they have fought to give new hope to those in despair. Even after entering prison, they continue to do such things. 

When I comfort those people and leave the prison, I realized that I cannot take on the mission of returning without leaving them a place where they can shed tears with a heart more sorrowful than that of a parent leaving their child. With that feeling, I moved forward. So, when I was released from prison, I saw many people holding onto me and weeping. Because of that, when I came out of prison in North Korea, there were instances where four people abandoned their parents and families to follow me.

Continuing that path, I came down to South Korea, pouring out my sincerity and true sweat in North Korea to gather the people God had left behind. However, when they opposed and turned away, I realized that there was still a path to devote my sincerity for those remaining in South Korea. Following that path in South Korea was not a smooth one. Everywhere I went, there were disturbances. Whenever I entered a town, fights would break out, and people would die. I have come this far through such paths.

And so, I met you and spoke… During the early days of the Unification Church in Yeongdo, centered around Chairman Yoo… The wonderful thing about Chairman Yoo is this: he swore that even if he did not listen to my words and read the "Principle Original Text," he would be grateful to offer his body as an eternal offering before Heaven. I met such a person during my lonely times. This is God’s work. At that time, the heart of the Teacher was serious. Because it was serious, God worked in that place. God works entirely. And so, I have come this far. I have come from the very bottom. Now, I have risen a lot.

Unification Church members bearing the responsibility for North-South unification
The division of the Republic of Korea into North and South and the creation of the 38th parallel is a retribution for not fulfilling God’s will after liberation. The desires of humanity
A person named A has his own hopes, and a person named B has his own hopes. Each of us has different personalities. Just as each face is different, we feel that our personalities are also different. Since personalities are different, the demands are also different, and the standards of goodness we desire are different. Some like this, while others like that, and in overcoming various environmental conditions, our living aspects differ according to our personalities.

Then, does having various personalities mean we must walk various paths? While each personality is different, the purpose we pursue must be one. Furthermore, the conclusion of that purpose must not be evil but good. The standard of that goodness must be absolute. And it should not be something that is only established in my lifetime but something that can remain forever. What we desire is not something that can be recognized in the changing historical era but something that can be established in the unchanging historical era. Everyone seeks a more valuable standard.

In our speech, we want to speak centered on goodness today more than yesterday, and in our actions, we want to act centered on more valuable goodness. Pursuing value in a place that can align with absolute goodness is our human life. This is true not only for our daily lives but also for our entire life path.

The purpose of the life I wish to achieve is not the content of a life buried in a temporary process, but rather, it is to have content with values that transcend history, hoping that the results manifested in that life will evoke responses in numerous historical eras, and wishing to leave behind something of more meaningful value is the desire of humanity.

Even if history changes, the standard of goodness must not change.
This world is a changing world. It is always changing and developing. Then, when we think about whether the goodness we currently desire and seek will also change with history, if that goodness changes with history, then the purpose or standard of hope that we, who live in this era, seek by pursuing goodness will also change, will it not?

When we consider this issue, even if history changes, the standard of goodness that humanity desires must be absolute. It must not change. No matter how much it changes, even if there are changes in environmental content, the purpose and conclusion must always be the same. In other words, when we view a straight line as the standard that humanity desires, there may be times when it intersects and forms a circle, but at the conclusion, it must converge on a common absolute standard centered on goodness. If that does not happen, then the hopes and conditions for happiness that humanity has been seeking until now cannot be guaranteed.

Therefore, while it is acknowledged that history changes and develops, the standard of goodness cannot change. Whether we proceed directly or take a detour around that unchanging absolute standard may differ, but in the results, it must be combined around a standard corresponding to absolute value. If there is nothing like that, then the actions of our conscience, which hope to affirm the highest goodness through the historical process today, cannot achieve their purpose. From this perspective, we feel that the absolute standard of goodness must not be absent from history; it must remain.

Then, who is the master of history? Is it humanity? Humanity is easily changeable. Yesterday it was like this, and today it can be like that. There is nothing. If we are in a position where we cannot seek absolute good or absolute purpose, we will face the position that we cannot find the standard of the highest happiness in humanity. In that case, we cannot establish a point of happiness that our lives seek and desire.

Where is the foundation of love? It is not within you. Historical Humanity

In those historical eras, there are historical periods centered around the world and, in the case of the Republic of Korea, historical periods centered around the Republic of Korea. While the length may vary, history certainly exists. Even within families, when we focus on individuals, each individual has their own history.

When we think this way, we realize that there is history for each of you present here today. Because you have lived through the past, that past has left an inseparable historical narrative with you, and it continues to do so. The historical narratives of the past and your present are not separate; they are connected. From the perspective of this connected present, we must reflect on how we have walked in the past and how we should walk today.

If the history I have walked is true history, then in the present, where I must leave behind historical facts, I must also be true.
