There may be differences in length, but if the past was true, the present must also be true, and the future must also be true.

What Will I Leave in History?  
From the moment I was born until the moment I leave this world, what historical facts will I leave behind in front of the Republic of Korea? In front of my tribe, or in front of my descendants, what values will I leave behind? This is something that, even without probing, will certainly be left in history. The question is whether I have left a good history or a bad history, whether I have left a good legacy or a bad legacy.

When faced with the final moments of fate without a future, if one reflects on their past history from the perspective of a present without a future, they must confront the urgency of settling their past. If one feels shame before their nation, what will their position be? If, at the end of their life, they stand in a position where they can regret before their parents, relatives, spouse, or descendants, what will their position be? This is a serious issue. When your life comes to an end, it is inevitable that you will conclude whether your time on this earth has been sad or joyful.

Regardless of whether one is talented or not, whether one leaves this world old or young, there are two issues: whether one leaves behind a sad life or a joyful life. Therefore, we must understand that we should weigh the past, present, and future and live discerning between good and bad.

The moment to discern this is not in the future or the past but in the present. The present is the moment of discernment. Today is the center of creating a good history. This one hour of living today connects to the moment that can determine the history of the past.

If the past remains a sad history, the present will also be engulfed in sadness. If the present is invaded by sadness, the future will also lead to sadness. When we consider where the decision between a sad history and a joyful history begins, it becomes a serious issue, and we must understand that the content that determines this is today, this very moment.

In this light, there is a path of destiny in the universe and history. There is a direction toward a certain purpose. There is also a line, like a horizon, along that direction. Based on that line, some may align at 80 degrees, some at 90 degrees, some at 100 degrees, and some at 180 degrees, adjusting their direction accordingly. The larger the angle of that direction, the shorter the person's path of goodness will be.

When viewed from the perspective of a single line, the larger the angle of the straight line, the shorter the distance to the line; conversely, the smaller the angle, the longer the distance must be. From this perspective, we must ask ourselves whether the life we are living now aligns with God's ideal of creation and God's principles of creation. If there is a certain line that God desires, we must consider at what angle we stand in relation to that line. Thus, we cannot ignore the question of whether we leave behind more joyful content or more sorrowful content in the course of history.

When does such a decision occur? It is neither in the past nor in the future, but in the present. Then, does good and evil get determined while one is just sitting still? No, it does not. Good and evil are determined through action. This is certain. It is not determined by sitting idly and merely eating; it is determined by one's words and actions, and the intentions behind them, within the context of their life stage.

So, what are the important factors that determine good and evil? They are our words, actions, and feelings. When we delve into emotional issues centered around our hearts, whether we feel good or bad, or whether we felt good or bad in the past, we find that everything from the past up to now culminates in the criteria of our words, actions, and thoughts.

If one speaks and does not act, can that be considered good? The extent to which one does not act leads to evil. However, if one speaks and then acts, it will certainly lead to goodness proportional to the action taken. The question is whether the action was done sincerely or out of obligation. Even if it was done out of obligation, the more sincerity is added, the greater the good that results, as we can see from our daily lives. This is a fact you all know well.

Therefore, when we say that we must walk the inevitable path of life that leaves behind a good history, the factors that can determine that inevitable destiny are few. They are our words, actions, feelings, and intentions. This is where it all culminates.

We listen to others' words and observe their actions, judging whether they are "good" or "bad." We assess whether a person is good or bad based on their words and whether they act sincerely or deceitfully. We must apply the same standards to ourselves. If we have the ability to criticize others, we must also hold ourselves to that same standard.

That is why the question is how much we act according to what we say. In our actions, we must not act without regard for our hearts or without concern for ourselves. The determination of good and evil hinges on whether we act with absolute concern, pouring our utmost sincerity into our actions.

When we consider all sensory issues related to what we see, hear, and feel, we must establish a standard for our words and actions, completing or reinforcing our personal standards. If there is something in our sensory experiences that can negatively impact us, we must recognize that it is absolutely yielding ourselves to evil, placing us in a humiliating position before evil.

If we cannot adjust to this, we will become like those who speak evil words, and we will find ourselves in the same position as those who act inappropriately. Living this way will inevitably lead to a sad history and a history of sin. When we think about this, we must avoid standing on such a standard and instead discern between good and bad, using our experiences for our own growth. If there are bad people, we must resolve not to become like them, and if there are good people, we must strive to become like them. Without this effort, we cannot leave behind good results in our lives.

What Believers Must Always Consider in Reality  
If you do not leave behind good results in your life, you will inevitably become indebted to the Republic of Korea, to your family, to your spouse, or to your children. We cannot overlook this fact.

The time when we can determine this and influence the entirety of our lives is precisely today, in this reality. We must not forget that this reality is like being tied with ropes from all sides and pulled. If the ropes are pulled equally from all sides, we can maintain our center at any time. However, if the pulling force from one side increases, the center will tilt. When the center tilts, the question is whether one can correct it alone. It is difficult to correct it alone when the center has tilted. If there is a way to correct it or someone to support you, you can correct it, but if you are in a tilted position, you cannot correct it by yourself.

You must feel this well in your faith life. Moreover, since we live not without purpose but with a great purpose at the center of our faith, we must feel this even more deeply. If the center begins to tilt due to a small mistake, no matter how much effort you put in, you cannot correct it. Once the center tilts due to a mistake, it is difficult to correct it even with dozens, hundreds, or thousands of times the effort. Those who engage in serious faith life will feel this deeply.

This is true not only in faith but also in worldly matters. If something goes wrong in the world, correcting it requires dozens of times more preparation and effort than it did before the mistake occurred, making it hard to return to a normal standard.

When we think this way, we must understand that maintaining a central standard without losing it and standing vertically is the most serious issue. The center does not tilt simply because one has a major conflict and is humiliated by another. The center begins to tilt from a single unpleasant emotion. If one looks at another with a certain feeling, and that person does not stimulate them positively but rather negatively, each of those feelings will feel unpleasant, and their standards will become distorted. This is how the standards for seeing and feeling become misaligned.

Therefore, if one misfeels or miscommunicates with another, there are many moments when they can quickly go astray. A small emotional issue, a single feeling, can lead to a deviation in your faith journey or your normal personal life.
There are times when it can be an important factor that can influence the problem. It means that my center can be broken because I saw it wrong. It means that my center can be broken because I felt it wrong. It means that my center can be broken because I felt wrong and spoke wrong. 

When God speaks and acts wrongly, you must have felt that you encounter decisively evil results in your faith life. This is something you feel not only in your faith life but also in your daily life.

Therefore, what we must always address in reality is to "correct your feelings, govern your feelings, and protect your feelings well." It means that you must have a special heart regarding all the feelings you feel emotionally.

So, we must do it correctly in seeing, feeling, acting, and speaking. We must completely determine the criteria that if you do this, it’s a plus, and if you do that, it’s a minus, and that you must not exceed this boundary line. You must not cross this boundary line. If you cross that boundary line, the public foundation you have built until now will be ruined all at once. This is something you must have felt a lot while living your faith life.

You are like a pendulum. If it’s a little too much, it goes up, and if it’s a little too little, it goes down. So, when does the pendulum stop? How do you completely stop the pendulum? This is the problem. To completely stop it, you must adjust the scale well so that the pendulum is horizontal, which requires it to go up and down.

There is only one horizontal point. The horizontal point is one, and it is so small that it cannot even be marked by the thickness of a hair. It is truly a long time to take a breath. During the time you exhale and inhale, the horizontal point of the world goes up and down. In the same way, your life’s direction sways based on an extremely momentary standard, which is a fraction of a second. Or it sways around a certain boundary line.

Even when you are on a boat, you must look at the direction indicated by the compass and go according to that direction, but even if the compass shakes a little, it sways. So, it seems that the compass points to a straight path, but it cannot indicate the true straight path. You must realize that this kind of play is being drawn in this moment, this time you are living. The question of whether it is evil or good is being determined in the current process of your life. 

Therefore, if you make a mistake momentarily, the past will all run away. If you make a mistake, the reality will be completely denied, and the future will be completely blocked by a cliff. When is this determined? It is neither the past nor the future. You must understand that it is determined right now.

You must establish a firm standard to repel the forces of evil. However, your standards are all different. Since each person’s nature is different, the standards you feel are also different. Therefore, you must pave the way toward what feels good to your heart, saying, “My heart should be like this. I feel bad at times like this.” You must say, “I will never do what feels bad. The time spent doing this is the time of dying.” In fact, the time spent doing that is the time of dying.

For example, when a person dies, they do not die suddenly as soon as they get sick. Death begins in a place where one does not know whether they are sick or not. That unknown place is the origin of death. There may be a temporal difference until the time of death, but since the origin of death begins from that moment when one does not know whether they are dying or not, whether they are sick or not, there will be a standard based on each person’s nature, saying, “I must be like this to feel at ease.” You must live according to that standard.

Just as there are many paths leading to a single meeting point, the destination each individual must go to is one, but since each person’s nature is different, the direction they take is different. Therefore, to walk the right path, there must be a standard that says, “You must not go this way.”

As a man, as a woman, as a husband in a family, as a wife, as a father, as a mother, as a son, as a daughter, or as a friend, there are boundaries. Since each person’s character is different, you must not exceed the limits of “As a father, I must do this; as a mother, I must do that.” When you exceed that boundary, evil will surely take root.

Once evil takes root, it does not perish alone. It always drags others down with it. It always tries to pull others down to perish together. This began when Adam and Eve fell. Evil does not intend to perish alone; it always tries to drag others down with it. Good, on the other hand, tries to perish alone. Centered on love, it says that even if I die, you must live. This is different from evil.

In a parent-child relationship, if it starts with evil, as the father and child become evil, the parent-child relationship itself becomes evil. Therefore, you must establish clear regulations in your daily life.

In your faith life, centered on God, you must set a standard saying, “I will not go any other way. I will not cross this boundary.” This is absolute. I can go freely to the right side, which is on God’s side, but when I go to the other side, I must analyze and critique it with utmost seriousness, more than ever, and be able to deal with evil as evil. To do that, you must have the conviction that you can overcome any difficult problem that leads to the boundary line and establish a firm foundation for your life that decides not to get caught up in evil. Otherwise, your life will not remain as a good life.

If we regard God as being in the position of a father and ourselves as being in the position of sons and daughters, we must be able to say, “As a child of God, I will not walk any path beyond this.” You must be able to say that you will absolutely not go to the left. There must be something like that. There must be a line, and there must be an angle. You must understand that the most important issue is how to align with that direction as you advance toward your goal and how to minimize the difference in angle. 

When can such a decision be made? It is neither the past nor the future; it is the present. 

Then, what attitude is needed in front of that standard? What is needed here is honesty. Be an honest believer. You must be honest. “I am like this. My heart is like this. Father, I will be honest, so please be honest with me too. How honest have you been with me from a position based on justice? Since I am in a position with an unjust heart, you may also approach me with an unjust heart, but now I want to approach you with what is in my heart, so please judge me based on justice.” You must be able to say this. You must have felt that this kind of heart is absolutely necessary as you have gone through years of faith life.

You must admit your mistakes when you have made them. If you have made a mistake worth ten, do not say, “Father, I made a mistake worth eight.” You must not do that. You must be honest before God, who sees your mistake as ten. Even if God sees your mistake as ten, if you feel like you have committed a million sins and feel pain, standing in the position of “I am someone who cannot be accepted before you, so please distance yourself from me,” what will happen? If you do that, you can communicate with God as much as you want. Even if God sees your mistake as ten, if you feel too honest and feel a million pains, saying, “I have no face to face God,” and try to run away, you cannot run away. Rather, if you stand in that position, you can receive God’s mercy. Isn’t that so?

If God sees your sin as ten, but you feel the guilt of a million sins and suffer, you can receive grace because of that. Therefore, there is no need for excuses before God. Since God sees honestly, you must be honest, saying, “I am like this.” You must feel that this is more necessary than anything else.

Some people, even after making mistakes, have many excuses. That is not being honest. When looking at whether the standard of honesty is one set by oneself or one set publicly, those who make excuses are setting their standards based on their own hearts, not based on public standards. Those who set their standards based on public criteria remain.

From this perspective, when you deviate from this attitude of life, you will encounter results that you cannot even imagine. Moreover, those who have had serious spiritual experiences have often felt that they had to repent for more than a week because of a single wrong word. There are also cases where one must repent for more than a year for atonement. Words are that frightening.

Therefore, whether in friendships, parent-child relationships, or in marriage, there are things you must do. If everyone you interact with is going in different directions based on their inherent standards, you must set a standard that says you will not exceed this boundary.

If you get swept away here, it is neither this nor that, neither good nor evil. God does not need that. You must be either hot or cold; you cannot be lukewarm. Therefore, those who commit evil and regret it can return to the good path. However, those who make excuses while being in a bad place can never escape that place.

That is why honest living is necessary. You must be honest. Honest faith life is absolutely necessary. We must be honest in our church life as well. However, there are many excuses. Nowadays, among the evangelists who have gone out to evangelize, there are those who have returned while evangelizing, and when the family asks, “Why did you come back?” they have many excuses.

In the Unification Church, the entire church must move together in the process of restoration that individuals cannot achieve alone. Individuals must go together with their families. This is the way to enter the kingdom of heaven. Families cannot go alone either. Families must go together with the church. Moreover, the church must go together with the nation to enter the heavenly kingdom. This is the principle.

Then, what is the more honest path? You must be honest before something greater. You must be honest before the nation, which is greater than the tribe, so even if you have a tribal perspective, you must not advocate only that. You must not say that we should do this based on our tribal perspective. The tribal perspective must yield and be absorbed by the greater national perspective. Even if the nation imposes sanctions on the tribe, the tribe must be sanctioned as a principle. That is the valid principle. The smaller issues must be absorbed around the larger issues. That is the principle.

Therefore, no matter how high the individual perspective is, the family perspective is higher than the individual perspective. The perspective of the family is higher than the perspective of the tribe, the nation, and the world. Even if the Republic of Korea has established a heavenly nation, it cannot have a heavenly nation of only the Republic of Korea. It must establish a global heavenly nation. To do this, it must become a people who can transcend the national sentiments of the many ethnicities of the world. There can be no objection to this. Therefore, those who have a broader perspective and can match their contents to that perspective and can harmonize in any environment will surely remain as good people. Those who cannot do so will surely stop along the way.

The path that our Unification Church must take is to prioritize the family over the individual, the tribe over the family... We must sacrifice the individual to find the family, sacrifice the family to find the tribe, sacrifice the tribe to find the nation, and sacrifice the nation to find the world. This is how it is fundamentally structured.

A person who has devoted themselves to the nation may say, “Aren’t I dignified in front of the world?” They may be dignified in the Republic of Korea centered around the nation, but they are not dignified in front of the world. When one becomes dignified before the world, the next goal is to reach God centered on the world. Therefore, when viewed from the perspective of God’s will, the world and God are one. Centered on the will, God and the world must become one. Additionally, that nation must always be one with the world. Making this happen is the direction the Unification Church must take today. This is the direction that the Unification Church must go.

If you realize you have done wrong, you must be humble. You must acknowledge your mistakes and say, “That’s only natural.” When you know you have made a mistake, there is no need for explanation. Your conscience has already judged and decided, so you know well. When you have done something wrong, your heart must feel shame. You must feel a sense of intimidation. Even if no one explains it, you know what you have done wrong. Yet, if you continue to make mistakes, you will face dire consequences.

When you realize you have made a mistake, you must be humble. You must recognize your shame and admit your mistakes. You should do that, but if you end up making excuses and trying to be shameless, you will not last long. As you go on, you will reach a destination that has nothing to do with you, and even if you are told not to part, you will part ways. After parting, you will not be able to meet again. Those who have separated by making excuses cannot return to the place they were before, no matter how many times they exert themselves to meet the conditions of those excuses.

This is because good and evil are fundamentally different. They are distinctly different. The positions of good and evil are clearly different. When one realizes they have done wrong, they cannot confidently assert, “Am I not like you?” before a good person, and naturally, they bow their heads. Why is that? It is because the position of someone who must receive the consequences of evil is in a different place, that is, within the realm of evil’s intrusion. Therefore, when one does wrong, they feel shame. That is inevitable. No matter how shameless a person may be, their conscience will feel that.
Because I cannot deny this feeling, I suffer even in the spiritual world. If this feeling did not exist, if I had not felt this, what pain would there be in the spiritual world? There would be no pain. However, because there is a feeling, you must understand through your faith life that there is suffering even in that world. 

Faithful people, sincere individuals, those who strive to live truthfully, know that if they say even one wrong word, it affects them. Their facial expressions change. Their eyes change. They realize immediately. In front of such people, even if one has lived loudly in the world, they become uncomfortable without knowing why. Even if that person is not thinking about it, the closer they get to that person, the more uncomfortable they feel. Why is that? It is because the levels of good and evil are different. You must understand this.

To resolve such uncomfortable situations, one must honestly confess about oneself. One should say, “I am originally this kind of person.” Honestly confessing, “I am a bad person like this, but you are a good person, so if there is a way to seek a path for someone like me, please show me kindness.” In other words, when you approach others with a prayerful heart, a free environment opens up. However, if you just stand there stubbornly, no matter how much you try, your heart will not be settled. You cannot resolve the environment and move forward. Therefore, you must honestly confess, “I want to relate to you as this kind of person. So please show me compassion.” That is prayer, prayer.

What is prayer? Prayer is what guides me to the right direction when I am going the wrong way. This play... When you look at your life, you are swaying back and forth due to one word, one action, one feeling. You are living this way. You must clearly feel that you are weighing this in the reality of today, in this moment where you are breathing and living.

To align that scale, you must be honest. For this (the scale) to achieve balance, the scale string should not be thick. It should be very thin. And you should not place the scale string askew. If you do, that is deception. It must be perfectly aligned. You must be honest enough to point to the exact measurement.

How honestly have you worked? Everything is related to this issue. Therefore, you must be more honest. You must be honest about your family more than about yourself. You must be honest about the church more than about your family, honest about the nation more than about the church, honest about the world more than about the nation, and honest before God more than about the world. Ultimately, you must go before God. One cannot say that being honest only with oneself is enough to go before God. One cannot say, “I have lived a conscientious life, so I can be proud wherever I go.” That conscientious life is centered around oneself, and no matter how much one lives that way, they cannot leave a plus in front of the nation and the world. Such a person lives in debt to the nation and the world.

Then what kind of person is a saint? A saint is someone who, with a single law, a single heavenly principle, always weighs their heart against the direction and boundaries of that principle. In other words, they walk with the world or with God, weighing their hearts and eliminating all guilt, and instead feel happiness that others do not feel while living with guilt. Therefore, saints are global figures. They do not live only for their own country or their own ethnicity. Isn’t that right? They live with a global mindset and a global way of life, which is why they remain in history. Thus, saints have been nurturing the history and traditions of the world from the position of subjectivity, spiritually and ideologically. That is a fact.

From this perspective, one must be honest. If there are two people who are not honest, a conflict will arise. A conflict cannot help but arise. They must be honest, but if they are not, they will inevitably face judgment. Then who judges? It is a third party who judges those two people who were not honest and were whispering happily. They may avoid that person and hesitate to be around them, but even if the two of them are whispering together, the one who did not speak out and did not establish a relationship will end up judging them. You have experienced such situations, haven’t you? When you feel bad and end up fighting with someone, it is a third party who makes the judgment. Such situations arise.

Now, look. Such relationships also occur among you. When you are living your faith and talking to each other, if you do not speak honestly according to absolute principles, the honest person will judge. That place is God’s place. God is present in such a place. If you cannot speak openly before God, who is the subject of honesty, and instead act in secret, whispering about this and that, then who will you be judged by? You will be judged by God. It is the same. A third party will judge you from the position of a judge.

Isn’t it the same in the world? If you commit a crime, witnesses are needed, right? That’s right. How is a crime determined? Of course, it can be determined by the words of the parties involved, but it is based on the words of witnesses. The position of that witness is God’s position. Once those two people start talking, it becomes clear whether their words are honest or not. Being honest connects with the truth. To be honest means to guide correctly. Isn’t that so? It means to lead straight. In front of that standard of being straight... If you start whispering, you become an enemy of God. You do not stand in a relative position to God, but rather in an opposing position. Who establishes the standard of judgment proportional to that angle? It is automatically established. Thus, who judges? God judges.

When two people fight, a third party makes the judgment. When two people fight, each claims they are right. The judgment is made by a third party.

Therefore, when you live your life centered on body and mind, you are never alone. When living centered on body and mind, there is always a third party. There are standards such as laws, social customs, or moral views. Those standards serve as the balance that can replace God. When you do not align with these, you will inevitably face judgment. Because we humans live within such a realm, our lives cannot be anything but serious. No matter how much effort one puts in for ten years, if they make one mistake, all that effort can be lost in an instant.

Let me tell you something. When you spend a long time in prison, the thing you miss the most is food. It may not be the case nowadays, but didn’t people who served in the military in the past say that food was what they missed the most? In prison, they miss food more than their mother, father, wife, or children. After eating, they feel full and then miss it; when they are hungry, all longing disappears. When hungry, food appears with omnipotent power. How great is the power of food? You will only know if you experience it. There are times when you are so hungry that you lose consciousness. When someone next to you is eating, you may only see the food and not the person. Such stories may not be easily understood. Those who have not experienced it will not know. Even when a person is alive and awake, if they have food, they may only see the food and not the person. Even if there is a person, their chopsticks may reach for someone else’s food. When they realize that there is a master present, the feeling of humiliation and misery is something you cannot understand. If one does not feel that pain greater than longing for food, they will always engage in such play. Eventually, they will be criticized by everyone. If they realize that they are reaching for food with chopsticks and that there is a master, the internal feeling of humiliation and misery is something that cannot be felt even with countless pieces of food, which is why they cannot do it again.

This shows that in the matter of good and evil, to atone, one must reach the highest level; without entering the core, one cannot completely turn away from that matter. The teacher has felt this, which is why when he sees someone in such a position, it is astonishing. Therefore, when debts come in, he gives them to those people. That is how he finds peace of mind; otherwise, he cannot bear to see that person. Acting this way brings a sense of relief to the heart. Unless one stands in a position where they have atoned many times over with material conditions, they cannot be liberated in their heart. If they do not do that, they cannot escape the bondage of the heart. To escape this bondage, one must atone many times over. Of course, to atone materially and temporally, one must go through a tedious period.

Sometimes, due to one wrong word, one may have to endure not just a week but several months. You have likely felt such things in your life.

Among colleagues, between teacher and student, or within families, see if there is anyone who likes to make excuses. When something happens to you, do you not try to pull others into it by saying, “So-and-so did this, and my younger sibling did that”? They say, “Why am I the only one being scolded?” This is falsehood. If one has made a mistake, they should be honest, but instead, they try to drag others into it. This is depravity. Therefore, in daily life, one must be honest. Before God, one must be even more honest.

From this perspective, in today’s Unification Church, the teacher must be honest while moving the whole community centered around you. The teacher must teach you from the most honest position. That is undeniable. If the teacher were to teach you for their own benefit, they could not endure it in their conscience. It is about teaching honestly.

If the teacher has taught you this way but you cannot act upon it, the responsibility lies not with the teacher but with you. When someone above gives something, the one below must accept it. If it is something bad, one can protest, but if it is something good, one must accept it gratefully. When teaching the path of restoration for families rather than individuals, one should accept it with gratitude. When teaching the path of restoration for tribes, nations, and the world, one must accept it with gratitude. When teaching the path of being loyal for the Republic of Korea, one must be especially grateful. When teaching the path to be loved by God for the world, one must be grateful because it is the most precious thing.

A person who is loyal to the world and fulfills their responsibilities before God is a person who can stand tall before their nation, their ethnicity, their family, and anyone. They can stand confidently before a mirror and look at themselves. They can praise themselves with an honest conscience.

“If I have done this much, I cannot do more. No matter how I look at it, I cannot do more. I have done my utmost until death. I cannot do more while I am on this earth. I have poured all my energy and sincerity into this. If there is one thing I have not done, it is that I could not bring this nation, this country, and the world before God with me. If that is a sin, then it is a sin, but I have done all that I could.” If there is someone who can go from such a position, that person will surely leave something in history.

Even if a person does not become prominent in the environment of that time, they will not disappear. God will ensure that the world inherits that person’s thoughts or that their descendants will bear fruit from that person’s value. God has that responsibility. If that person does not bear fruit, God will ensure they at least become a seed. One or the other will happen. Even if that person cannot stand in a position to welcome joy as a fruit, if they are sown as a seed, their descendants will surely reap the harvest. Even if they do not strive to gather, because God exists, the tradition and thoughts of that person, as well as their good deeds, cannot be denied. If God were to deny that, then God’s will could not be fulfilled. Therefore, it must be God’s will to cultivate, nurture, and leave behind such a foundation, and as long as God exists, descendants who inherit that person’s tradition or those who hold that person’s thoughts will surely dominate this world.

From this perspective, who should cultivate the honest attitude of a faithful believer? Let’s cultivate it starting from good people! That sounds good. Then, when looking at the family, who is the best person? It is the mother and father. Next, who is it? It is the older siblings. Then who? It is one’s wife and children. It goes like this. However, if one only likes good people, it may be good for the whole, but it cannot be something to boast about. Who would they boast to? To whom? Liking one’s own family members is something everyone does naturally, isn’t it? Isn’t that so? Liking one’s parents is not something to boast about. Liking one’s siblings is not something to boast about. Even if one were to say, “Ah! I liked my parents and siblings this much, so I am global,” they cannot become global. That is familial. No matter how much they may have achieved, they can only be a good child. Even if they did well... that is not something special; it is something that should naturally happen.

Goodness is revealed. It is elevated. The higher it is revealed, the more substantial the content one can boast about. For goodness to rise, it cannot be in an environment that is simply good. It must be in an opposing environment. If there is someone who can achieve goodness with a value that can be realized in a good environment and someone who can achieve goodness after working a million times harder, the one who worked a million times harder to achieve goodness is more precious than the one who achieved goodness in a good environment. They are valued more than someone who can achieve goodness with a value in a good environment.
If you think that God must love humans because they are His sons and daughters, then the problem is already solved. "Since God loves His children, what is good? It's only natural..." This is one way to look at it. One could also say, "It is natural for God to love us and for us to love God." However, God's position in loving us is different; we are the children of fallen enemies. Nevertheless, it is a source of pride that God, who is the subject of multidimensional goodness, loves us. "Even though we are the children of enemies whom God cannot eternally face, and it is principled to treat us like enemies, He has denied this principle and presented another, which is why I have become good, and I feel that I can make others good as well. Therefore, I can establish another principle and act upon it, creating a good environment. When I see that I have this heart for heaven, I must leave behind someone who can also have such a heart for themselves." This is the mindset one can have. It is not an easy task. To achieve this, I must make sacrifices.

That is why the path of goodness cannot simply be realized as it is. It is not achieved by good people liking each other. The call for honesty is necessary for compromise in a confrontational relationship, not to stand in an absolutely compliant position, but to stand in a relative position.

From that perspective, we fallen people must be honest. We must see things honestly. We must speak honestly. Perjury does not work. Therefore, the leaders of our Unification Church, those guiding the members, must put in more effort than the members themselves. If a leader has not put in more effort than the members, if they have slept even one hour more than the members, they should feel sorry and have a heart to care for them. Even so, if they say, "In name, I am the church leader, and you are the congregants, so you must follow my guidance," this is something that only robbers do. Does not conscience know this? 

These days, I think about what kind of people will emerge from our Unification Church when we have a lot of money in the future. I sometimes think it would be nice to give someone money for a year without checking the accounts. What would happen if one day I asked for the accounts? Wouldn't that person just make up some figures to match the accounts? Would that work? It won't work. There is no one to close that gap. When that happens, it is a downfall from something great.

The issue of work and mindset
I felt this yesterday as well. I gave some money to one of our members to do some work. The money that the teacher pays you is significant money. It is public money among public funds. If you are unable to fulfill your responsibilities with that public money, you can report to the teacher and use it for a second purpose and be forgiven. However, they handled it arbitrarily without reporting. I tried to forget about it, but the spiritual world said that this person cannot be trusted. So, I am thinking about it now. One must not deceive. The teacher does not like it when you think he gives without remembering. You might think that the teacher can be used whenever you need him, but he is not someone who can be used. Even if you try to use the teacher, he will not be used. Go ahead and try; who will fail? If you continue as you are, everything will have to be compensated again.

Thus, one must be honest. If you take money from the teacher and later come back with the accounts, and everything matches down to the exact amount of hundreds, tens, and thousands, how can that be? If that happens a few times, one begins to wonder if it is real. Think about whether that is possible. Is there some extraordinary talent involved? That is the problem. Mediocrity does not work. Moreover, the teacher stands at the forefront centered on principle... In other words, if the Unification Church has a global mission, the teacher walks at the forefront.

The teacher is currently building a temporary training center in Cheongpyeong to hold a principle seminar centered around established church pastors. Initially, they planned to set up a tent. However, after 6,000 years, the Unification Church and established churches are meeting for the first time... This is a once-in-a-lifetime opportunity in the history of our church. This is a rare opportunity. Anything that happens once is precious; the second time is not as precious. When I think about it, there is no money. But to set up a tent... Abel was taught to love more than anyone else in order to restore Cain by sacrificing his life, but I worried that if it rains during the rainy season, it would turn into mud, and someone might slip. Of course, if someone slips, it is their fault, but if they fall and break a leg or die, wouldn't that leave a stain on the Unification Church forever? If someone falls and hits their head on a rock, they could die from a concussion. Then, who would they blame for their death? They would say they died because of the Unification Church! Who led that event? It was decided and led by Teacher Moon! In that case, ultimately, they would say they died because of Teacher Moon! This is how it would be.

Last year, I didn't sleep at night while building the training center in Sutak-ri. I stayed up until 2 or 3 AM, wielding a club, and the young people were so exhausted that they ran away whenever they saw me. Yesterday, the person in charge of building the Cheongpyeong training center said, "Teacher, we are short on people." I replied, "You little rascal, have you ever worked 24 hours without sleep?" You can't say it won't work after eating and sleeping well. The teacher's mindset is different from yours. I would do it this way. My standards are firmly established. I guide you based on that standard. Your standards are different. Have you worked for 24 hours? If it doesn't work by 9 PM, you work until 4 or 5 AM. After trying that, if it still doesn't work, who will take responsibility for that work? If you have given them work, they should do it sincerely as instructed. But this is just a shiny surface; they go out in the morning and come back in the evening saying, "We are short on people." You little rascal... The teacher himself is working hard from early morning...

Yesterday, the sluice gates of the Cheongpyeong Dam were wide open, and a lot of water flowed out. For about 3 or 4 years, I have been going back and forth to Cheongpyeong, and it was the first time I saw such a large amount of water flowing out. We have put in so many stones for the embankment. We have been pouring our hearts into this, hoping for such a day, and now that the water has receded, we need to build the embankment... Until that point, we didn't know because we were building the embankment while the water was full. But now that the water has receded, the front is completely empty. If we widen this, it will expand by 70 or 80 pyeong. Stones are laid all the way down there. So, we need to build the embankment, but when I watched the people stacking stones, they were stacking them in easy places because they want to earn more. They absolutely do not want to do difficult work. They are calculating and trying to slip away like loaches, not wanting to take a step forward.

When the water was full, we had to stack the stones in a curved manner, but now that the water has receded, there are piles of stones in places where we can stack them straight, right? I thought, "Now it's done." But we need people to stack the stones. So, I took off my socks and stepped in. I have never stacked an embankment, but I taught them the logic of how it should be done. (Due to poor recording quality, some parts could not be organized.)

So, around 7 PM, we finished stacking everything. Judging by the sun starting to set, it must have been around that time. If we had asked people from the world to do the work, it would have taken them a few days. So, I commanded the young people, and in a rush, we stacked the embankment in an hour and a half, enough that the water could come in without any issues. But if we stacked it incorrectly and it collapses later, won't we get scolded? So, yesterday, I filled it with cement concrete. If we do the concrete before the water accumulates, it won't collapse. If the people from the world stack it, they won't apply cement, but what if ours collapses? There is a reputation to uphold. Also, proportionally, since we built it deeper, the chances of it collapsing are higher. If that happens, experts will say it is better for experts to build it, and that what non-experts built is not acceptable. So, I mixed sand and cement to make a cement paste and applied it. (Laughter)

When I see the workers, I feel frustrated. Their mindsets are different. That is why I do not leave them alone. Of course, even if the teacher stays quiet, no one will say anything, but I cannot bear to watch it with my eyes open. It should be done this way and that way, but everyone... So, as I said earlier, even the carpenters cannot move. It makes sense. "Isn't this how it should be? What do you think?" They say, "Yes, that's right." If they do it wrong, I correct it within two days. Then they say, "Oh, the teacher has come again." They might feel bad when the teacher teaches them, but I do not speak about things that do not make sense.

You cannot imagine how delicious the water from Cheongpyeong is. Moreover, no matter how dry it gets, it does not run out. Since it is hot now, when working and sweating, one must drink a lot of water. Probably, one person will drink about a bucket of water. I am also sweating on my back, but when I am working with a pickaxe, I have to deal with the water; what can I do? I just drink the water. People usually get diarrhea when they change water from their hometown. However, people from all over come to drink it, and there are no issues. Also, why do they eat so well? Even if I serve rice in a bowl as big as Baekdu Mountain, they eat it without even saying thank you. They have no choice but to eat well. They work hard, and since they have a lot of physical activity, their bodily functions become active, leading to good digestion. So, they work but eat well and drink well. If the amount of food is greater than the amount expelled, the body becomes strong, but if the amount expelled is greater than the amount eaten, the body becomes weak. When I saw someone who had gained weight since coming here, I said, "This person has gained weight," and they just laughed. (Laughter) They eat well, drink well, and digest well, so they become healthy. This is how good the water from Cheongpyeong is.

Building the training center over 90 pyeong was challenging because the site was small, and the well we dug had to be inside the building. We had no choice but to move that well, which was originally dug and covered with stones. I thought that since the cover was only about a foot and a half thick, we could dig sideways and connect a pipe. So, I prepared a budget and told them to make the hole. However, the person in charge came and said, "This well is buried five feet deep." I was shocked. I asked, "How could it be buried five feet?" They said they buried it five feet while stacking stones for the embankment. Originally, the depth of that well was nine feet... So, I scolded them, "You little rascal, is there any law in the world that allows you to do that?" How could the water accumulate if it is done that way?

These days, it has been raining, and a lot of water is coming out, but I wondered why the muddy water was coming out, and it turned out to be because of that. If the embankment had been built deep, the muddy water would not have come out just by leaving it alone, but because it was built shallow, when it rains, the muddy water comes up and flows out. I held the pickaxe and scolded them, "You little rascal, can't you think?" I had no choice but to dig the well again. How frustrating it is to have to dig it again.

Is there any law in the world that allows you to do that? How hard would it be to bury it and then dig it up again? If they had followed the teacher's instructions, it could have been done simply by connecting just one pipe. But... The members of the Unification Church are like that too. Until now, they have only gone out to evangelize, catching people but not actually evangelizing. Then, there are people who say, "I worked hard for three years..." What have they accomplished in those three years? There are many people like that. They are not able to make everything revolve around themselves. 

Principles apply everywhere. Therefore, when you go to work in a factory like a printing house, there is much to talk about. However, they pretend not to know. 

That is why, in the future, you must always work... The teacher's mindset absolutely does not work that way. "This work does not end here. I will use this here and then use it for something else next time." This is the mindset. When making one item, it must be made so that it can be used for two or three purposes. The same goes for building a house. We should think about the possibility of tearing down that house and rebuilding it later. However, carpenters only think about building the house and do not think about what comes next. That is why their mindsets are different.

What mindset would be good when looking at the overall problem? The mindset of the teacher is good. Looking at long history, we can see that countries with such mindsets have prospered. That is for sure. Therefore, I do not tell Unification Church members to do just one thing until they die. If you are a technician, you should be in your field of expertise. For example, if you are someone who holds a pen, do not think you will only hold a pen until you die. Can you live like that? Can you survive by doing just that? People may find themselves in situations where they are laid off or have to work in labor. So, try everything. Until you are in your 30s, you should try whatever comes your way. Even if you go out empty-handed, you need to build a foundation of skills that will allow you to eat and live anywhere. Even if you end up working as a restaurant employee, you should know how to cook well. You should learn the skills to cut vegetables like cabbage or radish in time with the rhythm. Is it unlucky for a man to know how to cook?

I say this. When I travel to local areas, I can tell how much water was poured for cooking rice, what seasoning went into the spinach, and what seasoning went into the bean sprouts just by glancing at them. I can tell how each side dish was prepared just by looking. But can I do it? Even if I don't particularly like it, I appreciate the effort put into the meal and say, "Thank you" while eating. (Laughter) I am someone who has lived alone for more than seven years. It has become a habit, so I do not need many side dishes. I only need one simple, delicious, practical, and useful dish. I always have a single dish. As long as there is one delicious side dish, that is enough.
is. That's why these days, when I see a table piled high with side dishes, it feels like a hassle altogether. When you go to the market, the side dishes vary with the seasons, right? A person's taste also changes with the seasons. For example, if someone eats Chinese food for several days, they start craving spicy and salty kimchi or radish kimchi. If they have to eat Chinese food again after that, it feels unbearable.

When I go on a summer tour, at every place I visit, the teachers serve watermelon and cantaloupe. So, just seeing watermelon and cantaloupe makes me go, "Oh dear." (laughter) Rather, I want to eat a bowl of cold soup made by slicing cucumbers without peeling them and adding seasoning to cold water, but who knows that? Therefore, one must know how to adapt appropriately to the environment. The same goes for faith and sincerity.

If a daughter-in-law stays up all night every day, putting in effort to make side dishes, but they taste bad, the father-in-law might eat them for a day or two, saying she worked hard, but after that, what is the effort worth? However, even if a daughter-in-law doesn’t put in much effort, if she comes back late after a little outing and simply sets the table saying, "Father, I'm sorry for coming back late," if she has prepared something seasonal thinking, "My father-in-law would like this," even if it’s just one side dish with barley rice, it can taste delicious. It can be that way. Of course, a daughter-in-law who serves with sincerity is appreciated, but a daughter-in-law who makes one feel good is preferred even more. Therefore, one must know how to match the mood. Being overly flattering is not good, but it is necessary to flatter just enough to not make someone feel bad.

God is the same. When praying to God with complaints, if you spiritually feel it, it feels like a heavy stone pressing down. However, if you praise Him saying, "Ah, God, you did well. I can roll from my toes to my head, and it’s all good," God will also be pleased. (laughter) Thus, while honesty is necessary, there are times when methods are needed to make someone feel good. However, honesty always works. Of course, there are things that cannot be done with honesty, and if you can harmonize with the sense of the times and the environment while being honest, there is no doubt about it.

I may scold you while guiding you, but when I go to the market, I sit down and joke with the ladies who have been there for decades. "Auntie, with a face like that, a nose like that, and eyes like that, you must be making a lot of money. Your son must look like this," and they are surprised, saying, "Oh, how do you know about our family?" Then I say, "I just know. If things go well, we could even become in-laws." And I know how to bargain to buy things cheaply. (recording briefly interrupted)

Tradition of Faith
When I go to Cheongpyeong, there are rumors that someone from the Unification Church has gone up the mountain. And those who are interested in me check whether I have come down or not. This can be quite uncomfortable. It’s not that inspiration comes from being inspired; rather, the environment creates inspiration. Just like a person who used to be a troublemaker must behave respectfully in front of many grandchildren, the environment often makes things uncomfortable. Sometimes, it’s not good. It’s lively. When lunchtime comes, they make rice balls…. There’s no need for a bowl. Whether it’s a pot or a pan, they cook a lot of rice…. If there are no side dishes, can you do it? Steaming hot rice, sprinkled with salt by hand, and saying, "Let’s eat!" is just right. (laughter) That’s good. It’s necessary in the pioneering era. Now, when I think about how to eat while driving, I start to have unnecessary thoughts when I see the teacher eating. When I see that, I realize that a well-known leader has many restrictions. Even if I blink, they ask why I blink. (laughter) When I look at the women, it’s lunchtime, so I blink to signal them to bring lunch, but others think differently. They have all sorts of strange thoughts. This is abnormal. Seeing that, I often think that I shouldn’t live like this.

Sometimes, I curse in public. I know that the benefits of cursing outweigh the harm. If I curse at one person in front of hundreds, people think, "How angry must the teacher be to curse like that?" They take it all in. If that one person becomes a sacrifice, allowing the remaining hundreds to avoid cursing, then I must curse boldly. The first-time visitors may not know and think, "What kind of teacher curses like that in public?" If you’re going to curse, you should do it stylishly. Complimenting is not cursing. It should bring tears to the eyes and make the heart tremble; that’s what makes a curse stylish. By doing so, I forgive that person’s mistakes. Do you understand?

When a prisoner is tried, the prosecutor demands a certain number of years in prison according to the law, but the judge considers the defense attorney’s arguments about the person’s patriotism or filial piety when sentencing, right? The judge can reduce the punishment or grant probation. Similarly, even if someone deserves to die, if there is no room for sympathy for that person, I might curse to create some sympathy and grant forgiveness. Those who don’t understand this will think that the teacher curses in public.

Some might say, "Chairman Yoo is a loyal follower of the Unification Church, yet he used to eat well, but now that he’s dead, he doesn’t get a reward, and he curses." Such people don’t understand the relationship between me and Chairman Yoo. We have worked together for many years; can everything be perfect? So, I curse in public to clear up the mistakes.

It’s not that I don’t engage politically because I can’t. If you try to deceive the teacher and live in double or triple standards, it all comes back to me. If you say everything is good while doing wrong, you will suddenly find yourself in trouble. God has made it that way. So, how well does God know that?

When I get angry, it becomes a problem for everyone. One person has the motivation and connection to influence the whole, so if that person is not managed, they can become a disease and bring harm to everyone. If that happens, who will solve it? When you can’t do it, the teacher must. At that time, the root must be pulled out. Therefore, cursing can be an option.

When you see this, there is a standard for everything you do. In working, when you look at the purpose of the work…. "Just because you say to work, I will do it; just because you say to dig because I ate today…." You can’t do that.

When digging, there must be a reason. For the sake of founding the nation…. The mindset must change. When that happens, the value becomes three-dimensional. From that perspective, if you say, "Heaven, please forgive my sweat and blood as a substitute for the sweat and blood of thirty million," it will be forgiven. It must be done in a place where God can recognize it.

To do that, one must not think of oneself. You must think from a public standpoint. Therefore, in personal faith, the traditional standards are not established based on self-centered criteria, but rather under public standards. Even when you leave a will to your children in the future, you must show something. "Children, be loyal to the nation like I was." You must have something to show. "Do good for others like I did." You must have something to show. If you have nothing to show, it won’t work. Therefore, you must have a public standard that can be good, recognized by others, and have the qualifications to be revered by others when you talk to your children so that they can also recognize it.

What to Pay Special Attention to in Faith Life
What you should pay special attention to in your faith life is to discern good and evil based on practical issues. When you step out in the morning, there’s no need for long prayers. "Father, as I greet this new morning, I must walk the path that is better than yesterday. If there are oppositions, please grant me the patience to overcome them. Let me not be someone who falters there but be a son who can establish Your dignity and authority. I will walk that path today. I will walk without hesitation. Thank you." That’s all you need. No matter how long you pray, if you don’t act, such prayers without results are useless. You need to know this and navigate well based on your current position.

You will die anyway. Raise your hand if you think you won’t die. Raise your hand if you think you will definitely die of old age. Raise your hand if you are young. You lack confidence. No matter how chubby you are or look like a pig, is there anyone who confidently says, "I won’t die before 80"? Didn’t someone from the Presbyterian Church die recently? Where did Mr. Seok-on’s old lady go? I heard yesterday that the lady who used to be so lively and noisy fell and was hospitalized, but she died. Is today the funeral? See that? Whether you die from illness or fall, dying is the same.

Thinking this way, can you confidently say you won’t die? Even older people can’t know. When will you die? Who knows if you’ll die with a spoon in your mouth before you even put it down? "I won’t die like that. I won’t die like that." But what if you die like that? You can’t be confident about dying.

When you look at your life, what will you leave behind? What will you leave behind? This is a big question. When you stand on this ground, can you stand tall? If you have done at least one good deed, you can stand tall, right? At the last moment of your life, when it comes to good or evil, you should be able to say, "Father, I am a good son before You." You must be someone who has that qualification. Such a person is greater than a hero who has the glory of a hundred victories and has transformed the history of the nation and the world. When that war is not a good war….

When Jesus died, He said, "It is finished." He is an amazing person. You can tell that there was a purpose in that young heart. Stepping over death and saying, "It is finished! It is finished!" means he has put in all his sincerity and effort, and he stands confidently without feeling lacking in setting the ultimate boundary of struggle, patience, and overcoming. When you see that, it’s admirable. Shouldn’t you all be like that?

The teacher is the same. When I get into a car, I don’t just get in. I mobilize the spiritual world. I set up sentinels and then get in the car. If I get in without such preparations and the driver does not match my heart, there could be an accident. If the driver aligns with the standard of Satan, Satan could cause an accident. Satan is always trying to attack me whenever there’s a gap, sending his direct subordinates to cause a crash somewhere.

When we offer a sacrifice to God, does God say, "Hey, I’m receiving the sacrifice now"? He doesn’t do that. He receives it without anyone knowing. That is something one does not know. Can humans know? God receives sacrifices in a way that no one knows.

Considering these issues, what if you die while driving? It can happen in an instant, so can you leave a will or anything? If you die without even having time to talk, what will you do? I think about all those things. So, walking is more comfortable than driving. The more serious the road I take while driving, the more serious I become than the driver. All problems are like that. If you die suddenly, what will happen? You’ll go to the spiritual world and say, "Oh no." Therefore, you must be prepared. Always be prepared.

Everyone Likes an Honest Person
I am teaching you principles and leaving a path to follow, but you must know that there is no forgiveness if you deviate from the principles. There is no forgiveness. If you deviate from the principles for some reason, you are someone who doesn’t understand. You are ruthless. The teacher has abandoned his parents and family. Therefore, I do not get swayed by personal circumstances.

I make the maximum effort I can up to a certain limit. At that time, when did I know that? That’s what’s needed. This applies to family, children, and to you. Just as I approach my purpose with honesty and simplicity, I want you to have that aspect so that you can be taken well to your destination. That is the teacher’s conviction in guiding the Unification Church members. You also need that.

I like honesty. The other day, Yoon Jong-young, a traveling speaker, came and reported. He was also in the Victory Federation, but he was just running around having fun. Not bad fun, but he was mingling with people from the world and attending parties every evening. If I left him alone, he would have gone astray, so I sent him out as a traveling speaker. The traveling speaker can’t even sleep properly. So, he has entered a path of hardship. You should have some sympathy for the traveling speakers.

Wherever they go, the Unification Church leaders are scolded, so I made him a traveling speaker to make him suffer a bit. When you become a traveling speaker, you can’t sleep. Can you go somewhere and say, "I’m tired, so please give me a room"? As soon as you arrive…. When you go on a tour, there’s no time to drink water. I know this well because I have been on tours. There’s no time to drink water. Can you ask for water as soon as you arrive? There’s no time to go to the restroom. The members follow closely behind…. Sometimes, you might say, "Let’s go to the restroom," when you first greet someone. It’s impossible. If you think that’s bad, you don’t understand. That person is bad, not me.

When they enter a room, instead of treating the teacher, they wonder if they can hear some news since the teacher has come. Rather than treating the teacher…
more interest in the news. However, if someone says, "The teacher came, but we didn't even treat him well..." that is fake. If you want to eat, eat; if you don't, don't. You just have to speak. You can't even conclude the conversation. So, that's not allowed. If you start a conversation, you must conclude it.

Then, around twelve o'clock, you end up eating. So, after having dinner around twelve, those who ate will clear the table and go in, but how can you just eat and then sleep like a pig? You need to work for about 30 minutes. This is how you always end up going to bed late. If family members are doing all-night prayers, you have to wake up early in the morning. You've entered a path of hardship. So, these kids must be more desperate for sleep than for food... Those who used to sleep well... I like the personality of Yoo Jong-young. He is honest. When he left for the tour, he wasn't feeling good, right? That's something the teacher knows very well. When he left for the tour, he didn't feel good about it, but when he went to the local area and saw the Unification Church members, even in their poverty, they were trying to serve with sincerity, and he was impressed by how they were trying to serve more than the teacher, who had sent them on a special mission. As a result, when you leave a historical past, even when faced with the final destiny, you will be able to complete a worthwhile life that leaves behind goodness. <Prayer> We hope that the path we follow according to the will is smooth, but we know all too well that such smoothness does not guarantee solid conditions for eternal goodness.

Father, on the path of restoration, we worry that just because someone called "the Unification Church" stands in a comfortable position, it does not mean that you can be at ease on the path of restoration. I often feel how insufficient I am longing for a comfortable today and tomorrow.

Even if the Unification Church receives the welcome of the nation and the world today, while Unification Church members may not face persecution and may have a free environment, those who bear the significant responsibility of leading the Unification Church do not have comfortable days. I have realized that the public path is always a path of sacrifice and inevitably a path of suffering.

Those who give must do so not centered on themselves but centered on God, giving on behalf of God, and must be in a position where they cannot help but give while laying bare their insufficient hearts.

This should be the case when going out with the word and in presenting actions. No matter how clearly the principles of upper and lower are established, that does not matter. If we do not have the internal determination to capture the hearts of those in lower positions and unite the feelings of those in lower positions to lift them up, the world of completion will not be achieved.

From this perspective, when thinking about whom God will come to find on this earth, I know that there is no one in the current Christian world who can do so. This group of unification is a group that the Father can despair of, a group that has gathered by the roadside, but even if they cannot act, they have feelings that they can sense in their hearts. They know what value they possess and what connections they have followed. When there is even one child among those who know nothing who knows something, we must know that we should place them before the Father, who wishes to find and meet such a child. Father, even if we have known, we must become your children who fear that you may take a sorrowful path when we are unable to act.

You have called us together and awakened us not to stand in such a position but to stand in a higher position where you can be pleased and where the traces of your glory can be revealed.

However, if we always cause you concern and always find ourselves dragged before you, we must think that we have not fulfilled the mission of being born as your sons and daughters. We must feel this more than anything else and, even if we feel we lack what we should have, we must struggle to prepare for that day.

Let us become like the heart of a bride going to her wedding. A bride cannot go to her wedding empty-handed, can she? She must bring something that can serve as a gift to her relatives or something that can be a condition for greeting. As we realize that we have been sent by you and that the more we look forward to the foundation of good glory on this earth, the more we understand that we are the ones you have sent, the greater your wish is, the more we must think about what path we should take. When we think about this, we realize that it is most frightening to grow older without being prepared and that it is most frightening when the moment of death approaches without knowing when it will come. If there is someone who struggles to overcome the painful journey, even if it is just by walking, that person will not perish.

Among the members of the Unification Church today, is there anyone who says, "I perished while believing in the Unification Church?" There may be individuals who perished while believing in the Unification Church, but I know that there are nations that have perished while believing in you. Believing is one thing, but believing incorrectly leads to destruction. There may be someone who stands here as a member of the Unification Church who has become the cause of their own downfall, but I am fighting to not perish.

No matter how heavy my burden is, I know that it is the responsibility of this child standing here to spend painful days thinking about how to digest your burden along with my burden rather than discussing my burden with you.

Even if I have something to boast about after acting, I know that I should not have a joyful day before you, who have not had joyful days until now, and that it is our path to leave that behind for the nation and the people. Father, if you love the Unification Church, please love the nation and the world you desire more than loving me.

This is the wish of the Unification Church, and you know well that this is the wish of this child standing here. 

Father, we must fight while appealing for the nation and the world. We must fight while appealing for the nation and the world. Such things should not be known only to us and you. Even the ancestors and descendants in the spirit world should know these things and be able to pray before you to fulfill the wishes of this son. "Father, is it not your wish to find such a son and meet such a son?" The ancestors in the spirit world and countless saints must join in and widen the scope of the connections that can cooperate with us.

Whenever I feel loneliness, you have always protected me.
