It would feel better to have five boats rather than just one, right? A procession of five motorboats going "vroom" is better than one going "vroom," right? Men, which one do you think is better? "It’s better when they go 'vroom'." Five going "vroom" is certainly better than one going "vroom," right? If we have a procession with five motorboats and the flag bearer holds up the flag, going back and forth from Cheongpyeong Dam to Nami Island a couple of times will automatically serve as promotion.

Then, you see, our Weekly Religion will not publish that article. Journalists from regular newspapers will come to cover it and publish it. Are newspaper reporters any different? If you give them a ride, they will like it. Then they will write their impressions and want to publish it nationwide, right? Will the pastors feel good about it or bad? If they feel bad, those people should be silenced. (Laughter) Isn’t that right? Among the pastors, there might be some who will ride a motorboat for the first time, right? I don’t think I would feel bad about it. I have a motorboat now, after all.

Three years ago, the teacher had a boat made, and while watching the boat-making process, I realized that I am not a boat-making expert, but I understand the principles. When a boat moves forward, I thought about how it would be affected by water pressure… When a boat runs, it pushes water back, so the back part rises. This means the boat pushes the water at a right angle, which makes it slower. However, if the back of the boat is wide, it can support more water, so the boat does not rise.

So, when I asked them to make such a boat, they all wondered what kind of boat it was. So I said, "What kind of boat? This is a real boat, so make this kind." They replied, "Well, we don’t want that kind of boat." So I insisted, "Even if you don’t want to, make it for me." And they made the boat. How much did they make? They made a 4-ton boat. Usually, they make 2-ton boats. Why did I want it that way? Because when I am busy, I need to be able to go out at night, and if I hit a raft, what happens? If it gets a hole, that would be a big problem. That cannot happen. Therefore, it must be sturdy. So I asked, "How big should I make it? Should I make it 2 tons or 3 tons? The biggest is 3 tons…" I said that a 3-ton boat is too small, so I told them to make a 4-ton boat.

When I asked them to make a 4-ton boat, the builder sighed as if it would be hard to make. I said, "Hey, if you get paid more, it will be fine, right?" (Laughter) So we agreed to pay more, and when they made it, it was so heavy that four people struggled with it. It was indeed hard work.

When it was time to launch that boat, the teacher thought about putting a 100 horsepower motor on it, but they put a 25 horsepower motor on it. The boat was this big, but they put a motor this small on it. (Demonstrating) When I tried to launch that boat, people at Cheongpyeong Resort gathered in droves, saying I was crazy. (Laughter) I was embarrassed on the spot. (Laughter) They said they would never go. So I said, "That’s your opinion. The boat will go. You won’t know until you see it." I got on the boat. Then people got upset and said, "What are you doing in front of our villa? Why are you invading our land?" I replied, "What invasion? Aren't you just upset because you want to oppose me launching my boat?" We even had a verbal sparring match.

Then I said, "Now, aren’t we going? Look." I got on the boat, and it was loaded with cargo. Just loading the cargo made the boat sink a bit. But there were six people sitting on it. So you can imagine how many spectators there were. (Laughter) Then I flipped the switch, and it went "vroom," and all the boats there started moving. (Laughter)

From that, you can see the teacher's discernment. The teacher's discernment is that sharp. Even though it was my first time dealing with a boat, it had to be that way. The logic is undeniable. It may be the biggest, heaviest, and ugliest boat, but it is the fastest. That’s the principle.

Be faithful from the small things. This time, I bought a domestic boat. I looked at it and thought it looked like it would run well. Indeed, it is no worse than a Japanese boat. A boat just needs to run well. What’s wrong with a domestic product? If it picks up speed, it feels really good. It doesn’t feel bad at all… How many times do I need to say this? To say it feels good, you need to say it seven times. Right? Is it nine times or seven times that it feels good?

To make three boats like that, can it be done without money? Boats are very expensive. Do you want to ride a boat or not? Our young people, don’t you want to ride a boat? Don’t you want to go to Cheongpyeong Lake and have a boat ride? Isn’t that right? When hosting guests, even leftover food is fine to eat. Do you understand what I mean? Back then, people who couldn’t drink milk could eat it even if they had diarrhea.

I made a good boat to host guests, but would I sell it after they ride it? Would I sell it or just leave it? I should leave it. Should I just leave it or use it? If I use it, who will I take? I will take all of you. Is that good or bad? That’s how it will be.

Is it bad that our Unification Church has acquired many boats because of the pastors’ public hearings? If we have eight or nine general-purpose boats, making a total of about thirteen… We are not just making one or two boats in Cheongpyeong; we are making the most at once. I plan to do that this time. Then, will the pastors feel good or bad? They will probably think, "Regardless of the Unification Church's doctrines, what they are doing is not bad." If it is something that feels good and is good for everyone, then we must do it. That’s why we are trying to do that.

So how much money will it take to do that? It will take more money than you think. Right now, how much does a boat that goes "vroom" cost? A typical motorboat costs around 1 million won. Do you understand? A regular motorboat that goes "vroom" costs 2.7 million won, 2 million won, 1.7 million won, 1.5 million won, and so on. How much money will it take to buy several of those? Will it not take money? "It will." But what will you do if you don’t have money? You have to buy it, but if you don’t have money, will you steal it? "I have to sell newspapers." (Laughter) What can you do by selling newspapers? You can’t do it even if you sell them for hundreds of years.

Ladies here, how many times a year do you want to treat the teacher to lunch? How many meals do you want to treat the teacher to in a year? Do you want to treat him to one meal a day, or not? Don’t you want to treat him to all three meals a day? "Yes." I’m saying you should only treat him to one-third of that. One-third means how many meals? 365 meals, right? You should spend at least 100 won per meal. Isn’t that right? You should spend at least 100 won, right? Ah, let’s have the teacher try some expensive lunch. It should cost at least 100 won. Isn’t a bowl of jajangmyeon 120 won? Would you like to treat the teacher to jajangmyeon, noodles, or cold noodles? You should spend at least 100 won.

If you do that, how much is that in a year? It’s 36,000 won. So you all need to save at least 36,000 won. Right? If there are 10,000 Unification Church members, that would be 3.6 billion won. That’s impressive. Our newspaper company expects to make about 4 billion won a month, so it’s something we can easily manage. The issue is how you can gather your sincerity; you should never think that you can’t do it because the teacher doesn’t have money. Do you understand?

We bought land in Yeouido that is nearly 15,000 pyeong. When we bought that land, we had enough money. Now, because the dollar exchange rate has risen, the current market price of that land is over 70,000 won. So that’s worth over 1 billion won, right? So now the Unification Church has become wealthy. Isn’t that right? Even though the ladies are going out and starving, they are starving to eat. Once we finish building the newspaper company, we might be able to wipe out all the hardships of the past, melt everything down in a furnace, and become a truly prosperous church.

I don’t know if you will gain anything from this, but whether the teacher is good or not, do you think it is worth cooperating with him or not? "I think it is." Since you have spent time with the teacher until now, you will think it is worth it. If you think it is worth cooperating, will you cooperate or not? "I will." Don’t start with the big things; start with the small things. If you say to start with the big things, everyone will fall off, and we can’t have that, so I am saying to participate and start with the smallest things. So what is the smallest thing? It is digging up the gravel field. (The rest is not recorded) *10)

Pioneer
<Prayer> Father, today is July 11, 1971. Please remember this day. This day, where 71 meets July 11, let your glory, mercy, and love be with all humanity, before this nation that has walked the path of suffering, and before all your children who are still fighting.

Moreover, tomorrow is the day we will select pastors who have gone through the seventh training session and start the public hearing in Cheongpyeong, so I hope that this day, corresponding to the 71st year of 1971, will be a new starting day established by you. We must fulfill the wish of the Father who has woven the history of Cain and Abel's indemnity centered on the church and churches. When I think about how we have now been given the opportunity to meet in a place where we could not meet due to hostility and jealousy, I hope this does not end as just a yearly event of the Unification Church.

Father, may you be with them wherever they move. Through those attending this time, may a new climate be created in the Korean church world, may we regain the rights of the chosen people that we lost due to not knowing your providential will, and may we be able to present ourselves before you with the original posture of the Third Israel that you desire. We hope that such a holy group can appear in joy before you, even if it is just one life, and you know our wish.

At this time, I believe that your little children are continuing their work without rest in Cheongpyeong. This is not work for the Unification Church, but rather a task done on behalf of the poor Cain-like people who have betrayed the providence in the established church and the path of restoration, so Father, please receive it in substance.
This work today, may the Unification Church, on behalf of the nation and the world, be accepted as a foundation for the offering presented before the established churches, just as Jacob did before Esau.  
Please bless your children scattered across the nation. May this day be blessed as a joyful day, and may it be blessed by the Father as a day of love.  
We must understand that before loving the nation, we must love our tribes, and before loving our tribes, we must love our families and individuals. Your children, gathered here under the name of the Unification family, must now adopt a humble attitude, reflect on the past, and, while looking at this suffocated world, hold hands and unite our hearts, feeling that the time is approaching for us to march forward as strong warriors of heaven.  
Regarding Joshua and Caleb, who were heading towards Jericho, the Father said, "I will be with you; I will not leave you nor forsake you. Be strong and courageous." Just as the Father wished for us to be strong and courageous, knowing the historical fact that the Father cooperated with us, today the Unification believers must recognize this time as a foundation for the mission they must take on for the world, raising a new banner and resolving to march forward as heavenly soldiers to defeat the enemy's world with one hand. May we become children who can pledge in our hearts that we must have a strong and courageous spirit, bringing about results of victory in every battle.  
History always has its peaks and valleys. We understand that it is the presence of these valleys that gives history its charm, and it is the existence of peaks that establishes the differences in value between what is precious and what is not. We must realize that whenever there are no groups willing to joyfully accept the mission of responsibility in any era, even the most splendidly historical nations will come to an end. We must clearly understand that even if there are many pioneers who have opened up a glorious history, that history will eventually pass away.  
Now, in this new historical process, the Unification Church has come to exist on this earth. All these connections did not begin according to human relationships but were initiated according to your high and noble connections. Therefore, in the depths of this, you are always present, and in the original direction, you are always at the forefront, guiding us. We must always feel and think about this, and we must become your children who strive to cultivate a serious and earnest self.  
Now we must be able to lay bare our hearts and express our situations before the Father. We must become mature children who know your situation better than our own and who can care for your sorrows more than our own.  
Father, who looks upon this three-thousand-ri peninsula with compassion, we must not become mere symbols of hope before your efforts and desires, which you have nurtured us for in order to make the final decision at the end. We must become the very embodiment of hope, the one organization that cannot be absent before the wishes you long for, and we must also wish for this as the Father desires.  
Compassionate Father, we must understand that you have called us out and led us not to bear fruit in the place of death, but to establish a nation that can praise victory in the bonds of life and to take on a salvific role that can save the world. Therefore, we must be serious about ourselves and realize once again that we must become true selves at this time.  
Father, we earnestly hope that you will bless this day. If we have not yet shed the appearance of a child, please do not withdraw your guidance, love, and protective hand. If we are mature children, may we boldly stand at the forefront and become the vanguard that can pledge to advance in a way that brings joy to the Father.  
Among historical figures, who has ever wished not to love their country? Who has ever wanted to abandon their kin? However, when the historical facts that must be left behind become greater than one’s own nation, one’s own family, or even oneself, we know that they have devoted all their efforts to deny those things. Today, we must also become your sons and daughters who can be filled with such resolve.  
Father, this morning, may you come and call each of us by name, asking what our wishes are, and may you show us that your wishes have a value that cannot be compared to our own.  
We know that the joy of one day cannot bring the peace of the end, and that the laziness of one day cannot guarantee the victory of a lifetime. Therefore, we must be diligent on behalf of the Father. We must be steadfast. We must not delay the mission of pioneers. We earnestly hope and wish that you will allow us to experience this in our bodies and minds.  
This morning, please look down upon us. With the gifts you have commanded, if we have had ups and downs in our lives until now, we must be able to smooth them out, and if our direction has gone awry, we must be able to straighten it out. For this, we need the Father. We know well that it is natural for us, as descendants of fallen human ancestors, to not expect the standard of ultimate perfection. Father, be our center, be at the forefront, and always guide us. Always be our standard. As a being that does not deviate, may we not bear the results of shame, always maintaining a good relationship with the center and the relative, and may we become your children who can possess the original beauty from a relative standpoint.  
Are there children who cannot attend this morning? Please bless those children across the nation who bow their heads and pray towards this place this morning. May all blessings dwell upon those who forget their own suffering for the sake of a day of victory for unification.  
People long for peaceful days, but we know that it is through the painful journey of working hard for the Father, rather than for their own comfortable days, that a foundation for victory can be established that will shine before humanity. If there are children who understand this, we earnestly ask that your abundant love may never depart from them.  
May your abundant gifts surround every place where we gather today, and may we be allowed to become sons and daughters who fulfill the responsibilities of priests without shame before the calling of tomorrow.  
We earnestly ask that you take charge of this hour and personally protect the young children who are on the front lines. Please be with your children who are fighting overseas, especially those who are at the forefront, responsible for the life of a nation.  
May all events remaining after July and all new endeavors we begin become the glory of the Father and the fruits of the Father’s victory, manifesting as an indispensable leading role in the cultural establishment of the new world.  
Please take charge of everything from this moment onward. We pray in the name of the True Parents. Amen.  
<Words> Countless people living on this earth all wish to live in a good world. It is natural to desire a good society, and everyone wishes to live their lives as good people, wanting to be honored as good individuals before a good society as a result.  
When we go to a certain region and observe it, if there is someone who is honored in that region, they must be someone who possesses a history that no one else in that region has. We know that only such a person can become an object of reverence.  
Even within a household, if there is a father or eldest son who is honored, that person must have a history that represents the family, something that the whole family does not possess. As long as that person accomplishes what the whole family cannot do and takes on responsibilities that the whole family cannot bear, we know that they will inevitably become the object of reverence for that family.  
Furthermore, if there is a patriot honored as a spiritual pillar in a nation, that patriot must possess something that no one else has in the historical process that the nation has gone through and must have faced adversities that no one else has faced. The greater the value of what they have left for their people to be proud of, the more that person becomes an object of reverence for that nation.  
When we consider that the history of individuals, families, societies, and nations develops towards a history of goodness, we must recognize that there must be many people who can respond for the world in the historical process of development. Such people must exist not just in one field, but in every field.  
To create a new culture that can expand the global foundation, those who take responsibility in each field must overcome the path of suffering to leave something new for the world rather than for their own nation. Thus, when the content of that overcoming becomes a standard that cannot be ignored in cultural creation, and because of that standard, a victorious environment can be presented, the person who has remained as such will inevitably be honored as the world strives for a victorious world and desires such a world.  
In this light, in the current flow of history, as many people sacrifice and work hard for the realization of a new world and the world of hope that humanity desires, those people cannot help but become objects of reverence before humanity.  
Therefore, it goes without saying that there must be global scholars, thinkers, and religious figures, regardless of their fields, who embody global content as pioneers. The more complex the responsibilities of such pioneers and the greater their missions, the more suffering will accompany them. However, if they do these things reluctantly, they cannot be people who can teach humanity a higher hope.  
Yet, no matter how great the path of suffering may be, if someone walks that path with all their life, and if there are those who leave behind regrets because they could not fully invest the mental or physical energy they wished to, even if they struggle in a miserable position that no one sympathizes with, and even if they collapse while striving on the path of suffering, we must recognize that even if their achievements are not revealed in their time, the ideals they pursued can remain in the future and become the spiritual pillar for those who continue the legacy of the pioneer’s victory.  
A pioneer is not someone who is content with reality but someone who challenges it.  
When we think this way, a person standing in such a position cannot be a happy person. They must shed tears of misery, and even if they struggle, they must do so in a miserable manner. Their life must be one that cannot end with that, and if there is a historical path of destiny, they must walk alongside that path of destiny. Because they cannot meet the day that brings them joy, they are in a position where they cannot see the internal decisions that can bring historical destiny joy, and thus they encounter the path of suffering on behalf of the future.  
Although they encounter the path of suffering because of themselves, that environment does not end with historical suffering or personal suffering. Because there is a spiritual strength that can surpass that environment, and because the remaining energy is rooted there, it is possible for the will to leave behind a new historical field to dwell there alongside that energy and root.  
When we think about this, we know that while many may desire satisfaction in reality, it is extremely rare to find someone who devotes their life to struggle for satisfaction in the future. This is true not only for our individual circumstances today but also when we look at the world today. Historically, there have not been many such people, and there are not many now, nor will there be in the future.  
Therefore, if there are pioneers who strive to inherit a new world and a world of hope, those pioneers must take on the responsibility for the future world that is to come. Furthermore, the more people there are who pledge alongside them, the more it is unnecessary to become someone who seeks comfort in reality.  
It goes without saying that someone who sacrifices the value of reality to pursue the value of the future, who devotes themselves and makes every effort, cannot experience the sorrow of defeat, no matter how difficult the circumstances may be. Even if it means that their own body may collapse at that moment, that collapse does not mean the end; rather, that collapse can serve as a motivation for a new restart, as we experience in our daily lives. Only those who stand in such a position can be called pioneers.  
A pioneer is not someone who is limited to affirming the values of reality, but someone who possesses the faith, worldview, and life view to affirm the values of the future beyond reality. In other words, they are not seeking something sweet within the realm of reality, but are in a position to challenge and fight to plant the values of tomorrow based on this reality. Only those who are not of such a nature can be pioneers. This is an undeniable fact when we consider the historical process or the circumstances of our lives today.  
A pioneer standing in such a position, a pioneer urged to fulfill such a mission, may seem unwanted by this era, but in reality, it is desired. Although this era may not seem to welcome them on the surface, deep down, it does welcome them. If such a person exists, even if reality does not welcome them, the ancestors of the historical era who collapsed on the path of suffering to fulfill such a mission and have gone to the spirit world cannot help but become allies of such a person.  
Even if they could not become friends of such a person on earth, nor could they become co-workers from all sides, even if they could not walk the path of unity in the present, those who think of such a mission cannot help but be allies. We must recognize that those in such a position are not only allies in the present but will always remain allies in the future.  
Why is this? Because history does not stop in the present but develops towards a better purpose, the ultimate foundation of victory, and the highest realm of rest. Therefore, in the process of development, those needed are not those who pursue their own comfort in the present, but those who invest their infinite value in the present for the comfort of the future. History cannot help but need such people.  
The direction of history, even if today’s environment is chaotic, will replace that chaotic environment with...
must have a higher level of commitment and determination to face the challenges ahead. 

In this context, even if the position of a pioneer is lonely, it is not truly lonely. When viewed from the perspective of the needs surrounding it, the life of a pioneer may seem solitary and miserable, but in terms of the substantive aspect representing the future, all people will admire him. Furthermore, the position of a pioneer, which seeks truth and strives for a higher world of peace and happiness, is never an isolated one in front of humanity. If he can feel such things, he will be able to overcome the difficulties that come from his environment better.

"I move history, and history moves because of me. Because I stand firm in my current position as a solid entity, the historical victory will come to me. Thus, while affirming the value of the center on the foundation of reality, I will advance step by step toward an unchanging and thorough ideology." If there is someone who confronts the path of suffering with this mindset, that person will not taste the sorrow of defeat even while walking the path of suffering; rather, he will become someone who can better feel the value of victory and personal hope.

Those who live this way cannot help but become historical figures. Moreover, if there is someone living this way, he will be someone that society cannot do without. We are well aware of this fact.

In the historical era, is there anyone who has stepped forward saying, "I am a pioneer for the world"? Even if such a person exists, if he resolves to escape the path of historical suffering and become a pioneer of history, he will be condemned by history.

Therefore, if there is someone who resolves to become a global pioneer and a new pioneer before history, he must be able to accept that path of suffering as his natural destiny. In overcoming a miserable environment, he must think of it as his inherent fate, and when he cannot do so, he should rather accept death as a better option. He must accept it as a matter of course rather than complain about it.

A person who has sinned must receive the corresponding punishment for that sin. If he has committed a sin worth a hundred, he must receive a punishment worth a hundred; if he has committed a sin worth a thousand, he must receive a punishment worth a thousand. It is only natural. When someone stands in a position where he has committed a sin worth a thousand but does not receive a punishment worth a thousand, and then complains, "I have committed a sin worth a thousand, so why am I not given a punishment worth a thousand?" there is still a way for that person to be saved even if he receives punishment.

However, if someone wishes to receive a punishment worth a million for a sin worth a thousand, or wishes to receive a punishment worth ten for a sin worth a thousand, that person will end with that sin. Moreover, the amount of sin related to that person will not be settled by him but must be settled by his descendants or his nation.

In carrying the mission of a pioneer who must endure the path of suffering, if one expects a certain amount of suffering and suddenly faces great suffering, and then complains, "Why must I face suffering that contradicts my position?" even if he claims to be a pioneer with strong conviction, that is where it ends.

However, even if one's current position is not a global one, when faced with global trials, if he can endure them and understand that they are an inevitable fate he must seriously bear in his life today, and if he analyzes and criticizes the trials he faces with all his efforts to digest them, then when the path of suffering worth a thousand comes to him, it will not lead him to ruin but will rather become an environment necessary for him to rebuild himself and inherit a broader foundation for tomorrow.

In this sense, today’s Unification Church members must establish a new history and be in a position to create tomorrow's paradise. At a time when humanity does not know where to go and is facing a grim wall regarding the world of future hope, every time they hear the sounds coming from the east, west, and all around, they must not only be filled with the conviction and determination to undertake the mission of a new pioneer that has never existed before but also become a group that marches to overcome such an environment.

Unification Church members must become pioneers of the new history. 

Young men and women, whether they are young or old, must face the conflicting environment of today as a natural environment and must not become a group that feels contradictions or conflicts in overcoming it; otherwise, God cannot have hope in establishing the future paradise centered on them.

While facing the current chaotic environment, one must think, "I have the responsibility to strike the decisive blow for tomorrow's victory," and must not allow oneself to become cowardly but must hold oneself accountable.

One must feel that the standard that the heart tells is connected to historical ties and that it is linked to the foundation of practical victory that can inherit the future. Moreover, one must realize that the conditions for victory that future generations, or descendants for thousands of years, will praise with both hands begin from today's reality, from under one's own feet. Knowing that every action and every aspect of the environment determines that, if one feels that he is marching in step with history, with the times, and with the future, then that person will never perish.

If someone tries to ride on him, that person will be crushed instead. If God exists, even if someone tries to push him away, the world of darkness will not welcome him; rather, the world of light will welcome him. Even if he is in a position of being pushed and trampled, it will not end there; it will become a new beginning where he can inherit a position that must be achieved without being trampled. We see that this new beginning unfolds amidst persecution and conflicting environments in both historical facts and today's circumstances.

When looking at a neighborhood, one can see that some houses prosper while others decline. In prosperous homes, one can see that the parents and children are filled with future aspirations. Even in an environment burdened with suffering, if the hope to overcome that path of suffering overflows, that family will prosper. However, if hope has disappeared from the foundation they have stood on until now, if future hopes have vanished, and if they find themselves unable to manage themselves due to a loss of realistic stimulation and emotion, that family will decline. Even if they are told not to perish, they will perish. When those people stand in a position saying, "We do not want anything less than the life we had when we were well," it will not matter that they do not want a lesser position; a greater position will not be granted to them. The more they do not want a lesser position, the more their environment will plummet.

We must clearly understand this fact.

In a prosperous family, when the father gets tired from working, the son takes over, and when the son gets tired, the daughter and mother take over. This is natural. If the father could not achieve his purpose after enduring ten units of hardship, the son must endure a hundred units; this sense of duty and responsibility, burning with mission, will lead that family to advance. If not, if the children do worse than the father, that family will decline even if they are told not to.

Just as one family is like this, so is one nation. No matter how great the trials that come to that nation, it is not a problem. They must declare, "Come, trials! We will surely overcome you and establish a new world of hope and paradise for tomorrow." Thus, even if the path of suffering proportional to that determination lies ahead, they must break through it and maintain their conviction to not stop in their steps of advancement. If there is a nation that is captured by the overwhelming hope of tomorrow, it will not be ashamed to emerge as a new standard-bearer in history.

However, if there is a nation today that has no hope for tomorrow in its current living conditions, but is only busy maintaining its current position, and if it sees the potential for that position to be lost and becomes despondent, blaming itself, that nation will perish, no matter how many people it has. Even if they are told not to perish, they will perish. When we think about this, we must realize that the future Unification Church is not the problem; the current Unification Church is the problem, and the past self is not the issue; rather, the current self is the problem.

What path must the pioneer take? 

So, what path will the Unification Church take, and what path does God, who leads and governs the Unification Church, want to take? When we ask this, God will not answer that He wants to take His children back because He loves them. The more He loves, the more He wants to lead them straight ahead. "Because I love you, I must not prolong the factors of suffering; is that not the heart of God's love? Does God not wish to shorten the path?" If we ask this, God will surely answer, "I want to lead you straight."

When God says He wants to lead straight, He is not speaking from an ordinary position but from a serious place. That serious place requires the resolve to overcome and break through all the environments of suffering. It is God who answers from the forefront with such a serious heart.

Then, if there is someone who knows this tedious path of restoration and is responsible for it, what path will he choose? Would he not choose the path that allows him to overcome in ten days, even if it means risking his life, rather than suffering for ten years? Since God wishes for it to be so, it is only natural that we, who stand in the position of sons who must fulfill such a mission, walk that path. There is no other answer.

So what should the Unification Church answer? While I answer this way, how should the Unification Church itself respond? If they have a teacher guiding them, they should say, "Teacher! Please come here. Your desire is such, and so is our desire. We have been hoping for this and preparing for it from the beginning." They must be able to unite in anticipation of that day. If there is a group that is filled with the conviction to await the final notice from the commander-in-chief and to advance in a full-scale assault, that group is not one that is united for the sake of reality. They are not a group gathered for reality but a group united for the future. If such a form is established and they stand in a position to overcome the environment, that group will not perish.

Currently, they are building a building in Cheongpyeong, and if the weather had not been bad, it would have progressed according to plan. However, now the rainy season is a problem. I expect it will end today or tomorrow, but even if it does not end tomorrow, the pastors will be settled. So even yesterday, despite the pouring rain, we had to purchase materials. It is not that there is a phone, and people had to go out and make contact directly. I had no choice but to go out in the pouring rain and take a boat. The rain was pouring down so hard that it felt like I was running away. It felt like I was in a position to avoid gunfire from a machine gun behind me. I thought, "What kind of madness is this?" Such things happen quite often.

The people working in Cheongpyeong have been digging for dozens of days. Even so, they can only sleep for about four or five hours. They are at the brink of death. Yesterday, when I said to send out the injured, eight out of 26 stepped forward. One-third were injured. So when I looked at their faces, they were not seriously injured. They were limping because they had minor injuries from a pickaxe or a nail. So I said, "You guys, someone needs to get injured here. Someone needs to shed blood." This place is a place of indemnity.

The Unification Church style is a way of pioneering everything. 

This time, I restructured the world into a new system and called all the people who were responsible for practical work in the world. These guys keep tarnishing the name of the Unification Church. So I thought I should make them work once, and I called them in a planned manner. So can they run away? If they run away, ten years of study will be in vain. So they have no choice but to stay put.

Even so, when the teacher is watching, they feel energized, but when I am not there, they feel drained. Why is that? When the teacher is there, they work even if it is night, but when the teacher is not there, they lose all their energy. Just by being here for one day and sleeping, I can turn everything upside down. So it is chaotic. Even the work of someone who has built houses for decades requires my coaching to be done properly. I am not even a carpenter.

Seeing that, it is clear that there is no such thing as an expert. From a serious standpoint, when observing the value of that standard, one can immediately tell whether it fits or not.

When laying the ondol, I have to coach, "The ondol should be laid like this." Also, yesterday, the people who came to dig a well asked me where to dig. If they are well diggers, they should know where the water will come out by looking at the mountain ridges, but they come to ask me where to dig. It seems that they treat me like a leader. During the days of work, even the carpenters made mistakes and got scolded by me and had to redo things, so they now look at me cautiously, asking, "Where should we dig?" So I said, "Where should you dig? How have you been working all this time without knowing that? A well should be dug where there is a boundary between hard and soft ground; when that vein flows straight and then tilts sideways, if you hit it along that vein..."
"It's water coming out, isn't it?" I asked, and they replied, "When did you learn to dig wells?" That's the logic. What have I learned? (laughter) That's how it is. You can tell just by looking at it.

As a leader who has been guiding the Unification Church until now, all the issues that have been resolved are now all formalized. You can tell immediately what needs to be done just by looking at it. Even though things are like this now, you know what the outcome will be. You don't just look at one place; you look at the whole picture. Even when preparing the land, you look at the whole and prepare it accordingly. Everything is like that.

So, the Unification Church style is all about pioneering. Building a house in Cheongpyeong, which should take about two months, is completed in just eight days. I told them to start preparing the land from the first day of July, and we began on the second. So, everything is done in a week. Until yesterday, we laid the floor and painted the walls, and then we finished the ceiling. If it rains, it can actually be a blessing. So today, we are organizing everything.

Seeing me do this, many Unification Church members say, "Well, the teacher must have a natural disposition that can't digest anything unless he does this, can't sleep, and has a strong fate, so it can't be helped. He does this out of joy, so there's no need for sympathy." 

The house built in Cheongpyeong is 93 pyeong. This auditorium is about 40 pyeong, so it can accommodate more than double the number of people here. Also, if we consider just the auditorium of the Cheongpyeong training center, it is about 70 pyeong, so it can comfortably sleep over 200 people. Such a house is completed in just a week. If we count today, it will be ten days. Today is July 11, 1971, but originally, it was supposed to be finished by yesterday. So, we must not go beyond today. Everything is to be completed in these eight days, and then we will do the finishing touches. We will paint... It will take about three to four days for the finishing touches. However, the finishing touches are not done well. Why? Because right now, it’s like going to a new house in a refugee situation. Even if you go to a new house without finishing touches, if you meet the groom, you can live well.

Humans have the qualities of pioneers. The Unification Church is pioneering. Even in building a house, it is pioneering. When we built the Sutak-ri training center, we completed it in 28 days. Since the ground was frozen, we rested for a week, so it was actually built in 21 days. We are creating history. If we are late compared to others, it feels bad.

Yesterday, when I was coming out of Cheongpyeong, I asked what they wanted to eat, and they said they wanted to eat, but more than that, they said sleeping was the best. Then, as soon as we had lunch, everyone collapsed and fell asleep. Recently, I bought 10,000 won worth of snacks and piled them up, giving them out once a day, but now that the work is done, I told them to take the snack bags and eat if they wanted, but not to wake those who were sleeping, and everyone woke up. (laughter)

For those people, sleep is truly precious. They can't express how much they miss sleep. Sometimes, even when it's time to eat, I deliberately instructed not to serve food. When it passed eleven, twelve, or three o'clock, one or two people would ask, "Isn't it time to eat?" When I said, "Not yet," they would laugh at first, but after a little more time passed without food, they would all turn their heads and look. Seeing that, I think the communist rationing system is incredible. Rather than talking about love, it seems that managing food is the quickest way.

However, if a servant of the master or a messenger does not know and is disrespectful, the master can see and forgive that. Isn't that right? Even though it is all for their sake, there are many complaints. There are many complaints, but these complaints are good complaints. That is how I see it. However, that does not mean I am burdened with a guilty conscience.

From this perspective, ultimately, thinking of their sons and daughters or their future, and in a broader sense, to save them, it is better that I do not meet them. When they say in public, 'Teacher Moon of the Unification Church, are you really such a famous person?' what can I say? There are various complicated issues. Because there are such and such issues, I am putting you forward to do the work.

Delegating the company to you is not because Teacher Moon cannot do it. The teacher is someone who can analyze human psychology. I often feel unsatisfied when I assign work to you. There are many things that do not sit well with me, but such matters are not my responsibility. It is not my responsibility to run the company or to be the chairman of the Victory Association.

I do not know what the future holds, but for now, based on the principle of restoration and indemnity, we must go beyond the national boundaries centered on the church. The company or the Victory Association is merely indirect and provisional means to supplement and strengthen the church; it is not direct. This is the Unification Church way.

You must understand all of this and once again prepare your posture to fulfill the mission of a pioneer. Now, you are in a position to fulfill the mission of a national, Asian, and global pioneer, so you must understand that you need to present revolutionary and new valuable content in all aspects, including your lifestyle and environment.

In that sense, during the summer of 1971, the 40-day evangelism period must mobilize everyone. It must be mobilized centered around families in a new meaning that is different from the 1960s. Thus, you must become pioneers in the face of a new mission and a new era.

Become a pioneer who leaves behind the value of life. Now, let us raise our hands if we are going to go out for pioneering on July 20th. Everyone must go out. I am telling you to go down. It is a principle that everyone goes out. However, if there are important responsibilities or positions you currently hold, that will be a special exception. In that sense, you must prepare.

Those who do not go out this time may shed tears in the future. This time, I might distribute a bundle of money to those going out for pioneering evangelism. Or you might meet the teacher at the local church. If you meet him, it will not be bad. You might take a picture in the local area. If we take a picture saying, 'This is a commemorative photo of the 1971 summer special 40-day evangelism,' those who have that photo may have a different future.

Back in 1961, I once distributed ten-won coins. If anyone has that, please raise your hand. Do not lose it. This time, I plan to take a good camera and take pictures. I want to make that photo a lifelong memento. At that time, the mother must also go. The teacher might do that. The photos taken during that 40-day period will be worth ten million won each, and they will be photos that cannot be exchanged for four hundred million won. Those will be photos that cannot be obtained except this year. I am thinking of doing that. However, I might not do it.

Knowing that, we must move forward centered around the year 1971 in a new meaning. Now that a bridge has been built between you and me, we can cross over. Everything is relative now.

Yesterday, I received a letter from China, and it said that pastors are coming in and worrying. They are coming in to receive training. Those pastors are eager to hear the principle words. That is restoration, isn't it?

Until now, the Unification Church has been busy evangelizing the lowest class, but now the upper class is coming in and causing a stir. In the future, there will come a time when they will want to hear principle lectures in the royal court. Who can guarantee that such a time will not come? It cannot be avoided, which is why Teacher Moon of the Unification Church has been doing this work until now.

You must understand that the sincere efforts and dedication you make in Korea can become a higher historical material that can move the world. Therefore, do not miss this opportunity and bring the value of your life to a meaningful result, and I hope you become responsible leaders with the mindset of pioneers.

<Prayer> Beloved Father, how much have you worked to lead this child standing here from the time of the helmet until now? Looking back on the many stories of the past and facing the complex circumstances of the present and the various problems that need to be resolved, I realize how fearful and daunting the mission is to go in the direction that you desire. I must not rise higher than you, nor fall too far behind you; standing in your position and following you is the path this child has walked until now.

Now is a serious and urgent time to inherit the heart of the one thought that you are worried about in the journey of actions that no one knows. Every time I think of you, who works with a heart greater than mine, I know that you do not blame the mistakes of this nation or the mistakes of the church, but rather, you continue to hold onto and move forward with the concerns for the future of this country and this nation through me, through the Unification Church.

If the hoped-for nation and the hoped-for church cannot reach an environment where they can be embraced in your bosom, how miserable it would be, and out of concern for that, you have worked to ensure that such an environment can reach us.

This is absolutely not achieved by the efforts of the Unification Church members. We know well that it is achieved by your invisible efforts. This child knows even better.

Father, you must take responsibility for the future fate of this church. I know that no one else can be the owner here. I know that only someone who loves this organization more than anyone, loves this purpose, loves you who established this organization and this purpose, loves the world you are concerned about, and loves humanity while overcoming the path of suffering can move this organization.

The fate of the Unification family is directly connected to your fate, and because it is connected to your fate, it must be even more directly connected to the fate of the world. When we look at this solemn task of finding the fundamental content that can influence the fate of history, we must become your sons and daughters who can regret our shortcomings and yearn to show the hopeful image of tomorrow before you.

We must struggle to break out of today's limitations and honestly critique and accept the conditions that remain for us to overcome our current miserable situation.
May the Father protect the future of the Republic of Korea. The workers of unification, with tearful hearts, are holding onto the divided North and South Korean peoples and are in the process of building an altar before the Father with new meaning, dedicating their efforts until October, which You are well aware of. O Father, who has compassion for us, O Father, who knows our intentions and opens the way for us, You are deeply concerned about our future because the content of Your story, which should not enter a place of ruin, is established both inside and outside of our humble background. We know all too well that You must establish a connection with us along with the nation.

Therefore, we understand that we must create an environment that can accept our ideology. We know that You have fought for us while overcoming the multifaceted path of suffering. We can only bow our heads in gratitude a million times.

Beloved Father, when You appear in the original form that You encourage us to take, we know that there will be no one to hold Your hand and call You 'Father,' and that no one will bow their heads and say 'Father' before Your glorious presence. Moreover, because You have come with the heart of a parent who sheds tears even in the lowest and most miserable places, we have become children who have developed the habit of calling out to You whenever we feel lonely. We have become sons and daughters who have developed the habit of seeking Your cooperation in times of difficulty.

You are the Father who must receive our glory, yet we must rediscover that You are not the Father who can cooperate with us in such a position. We must be concerned that our connection with You may be severed, and we must understand that even if we enter a place of death a thousand or ten thousand times, we must not lament. We must become the kind of children who can deny ourselves and elevate You, and we earnestly hope and wish to become such sons and daughters who strive and resolve to be so.

Father, how much have You longed for us to feel Your warm touch when we hold Your hot hand? Every time we held Your hand, Your touch was warm, but our hands were cold. You were our hope, but we were despair. You fought for us, but we made You bear the cross from a ruthless standpoint. We must recognize that we are those who cannot break free from the ties of our past. We must feel ashamed to reveal our identity before Your holiness, and we must realize that we can only call upon You while turning away because we cannot stand before You directly. We must also be able to lament that we have not become the sons You desire, and that we have not become the daughters You wish for.

We want to see You, we want to meet You, and we want to forget everything to move according to Your commands, running madly towards You. We must desire to act passionately. We must become sons and daughters who can spend the night in tears, longing for the position we have not yet attained, and we must clearly realize that this is the position of children with the tradition of the unification family.

If there is a history of misfortune approaching in the future, please let us take responsibility for it. If there are difficult paths in world history, we must become the breakwaters. We must be resilient, persistent, and strong. We must become a group of unification that is harder, stronger, and more resilient than concrete or rebar.

Reflecting on the path we have taken over the past fifty years, we must feel that we need to go forward with even greater strength in the path ahead, and we must also feel that those who follow us are a pitiful group. The longer the path of suffering is, the more they will resent. You know well the reason why the people of Israel perished during their 40 years in the wilderness, don't You? Therefore, please protect this pitiful group, Father. Rather than just looking at Mount Sinai, make them children who can empathize with Your heart as they go.

For this, Father, as they pray day and night without rest, please stimulate and lead them among the dreams.

Let us not be sons and daughters who face You with resentment while drinking the bitter cup of defeat, but let us be sons and daughters who can praise You with a heart of gratitude for the glory of victory and with a desire for compassion. In order for us to step into such a position, let this be a time for each of us to firmly realize that we must embody the traditional spirit of pioneers and find what can remain as a stimulus for tomorrow, and that we must diligently strive to fulfill that responsibility and mission in reality.

Please look over every place where we gather today. Moreover, Your sons and daughters from Japan are receiving training at the training center. The desire to see, meet, and go to the places they long for must be weaker than the desire to want to live here. Before the desire to return becomes dominant, the desire to remain here must be strong, and they must be left in connection with You. Please look over them. We earnestly hope and wish that they will return with more fruitful and hopeful hearts than when they came.

Comfort them. Please look over the family members in Japan. Every time I see them overcoming the path of suffering while standing at the forefront on behalf of history, I often acknowledge my many sins. The reason why we must make these foreign nations undertake such tasks beyond this nation is that we have placed ourselves in a position where we must push them into the path of suffering, the way of the cross, and the place of darkness without shame for this nation. Please be with them with abundant love.

They are those who claim to be the best nation in Asia. Even before You, they are worthy of being praised as sons and daughters representing all peoples of the world, so please allow them to endure and overcome until the end to leave behind a tradition worthy of that.

Please remember the countless children scattered around the world. In the future, may all the plans made over the next eight years be fulfilled within Your will, so that we can return to You with joy and offer ourselves on the day when Your desires are fulfilled.

I earnestly ask You again to personally guide and lead this place where we have gathered today. We thank You for this time, and I pray all these words in the name of True Parents. Amen.
